I.　To live out and work out the New Jerusalem to build up Zion as the reality of the Body of Christ requires spiritual warfare; at the time of Nehemiah, "those who built the wall and those who carried burdens took the loads with one hand doing the work and with the other holding a weapon"—Neh. 4:17:
1　仇敌有三面的攻击：第一面是仇敌的嗤笑（二10，四2～3）；第二面是仇敌借由神圣建造的毁坏者设计谋，要我们去开会，去讨论（六2）；第三面是叫我们灰心，叫我们软弱，叫我们生属灵的病，也叫我们不能同心（四10～12）。─引用经文
1.　There are three aspects of the attack of the enemy: the first aspect is the enemy's mocking (2:10; 4:2-3); the second aspect is for the enemy to set up plots through the destroyers of the divine building asking for meetings and discussions (6:2); the third aspect is to cause us to be discouraged, weakened, spiritually sick, and in discord (4:10-12).
2　尼希米是爱神的人，他在交通中祷告神、接触神；为着城墙的重建，尼希米站在神的话上，并照着神的话祷告，并且在复活里，在正确的进取里行事─一1～11，二4，四4～9，十三1～30。
2.　As a person who loved God, Nehemiah prayed to God to contact Him in fellowship; for the rebuilding of the wall, Nehemiah stood on God's word, prayed according to it, and was aggressive to take action in a properly aggressive way in resurrection—1:1-11; 2:4; 4:4-9; 13:1-30.
3　我们需要时时在灵里祷告，穿戴神全副的军装，用争战的祷告在身体里打仗，好站住抵挡魔鬼的诡计，以建造基督的身体作神的家，使神得着荣耀，并作神的国，使神掌权，而使神的经纶得着完全的成就─弗六10～20。
3.　We need to stand against the stratagems of the devil by fighting the battle in the Body with fighting prayers, praying at every time in spirit to put on the whole armor of God to build up the Body of Christ as the house of God for the glory of God and as the kingdom of God for the dominion of God for the complete fulfillment of the economy of God—Eph. 6:10-20.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第七篇　活在基督耶稣的心肠里，而活在基督身体的实际里（一）活在基督耶稣的心肠里并让基督活在我们的心肠里
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：诗十六7，歌五14下，腓一8，门7，20，西三12，多三4
壹　“叫众召会都知道，我是那察看人肺腑心肠的”─启二23中。
贰　我们若要活在基督身体的实际里，就需要活在基督耶稣的心肠里，并让基督活在我们的心肠里─腓一8，弗四16。
叁　基督成了人，就有人的心肠同其各种功用，基督在祂心肠里的经历，就是祂在祂心思、情感、意志、魂、心、灵里的经历，包括祂的爱好、愿望、感觉、思想、定意、存心和打算─路二49，约二17，太二六39，赛五三11～12，四二4，可二8：
一　平安祭牲的内脏表征基督向着神之内里所是的柔顺、微小与宝贵，使神满足─利三3。
二　基督的心肠在夜间也警戒祂─诗十六7下，赛五十4：
1　当神指教为人的基督时，基督借着与神接触，祂的心肠也警戒祂─诗十六7。
2　基督的心肠与神是一；这是神人正确的经历─腓一8。
三　“他的肚腹如同象牙作的，外面包着蓝宝石”（歌五14下）；基督的心肠（肚腹）满了深刻、柔和的感觉，那是在明净的属天景象下（蓝宝石─参出二四10）借着受苦所作成的（象牙作的）。─引用经文
四　吃逾越节的羊羔，要带着内脏而吃，表征接受基督内里的诸部分─十二9，腓一8。
肆　保罗是一个不断经历基督之心肠的人─腓一8，二5，林前二16下，罗八6：
一　保罗甚至在基督的心肠，在祂的情感、柔细的怜悯以及同情里，与祂是一─腓一8。
二　保罗没有持守自己的心肠，而是以基督的心肠为他的心肠─弗三17：
1　保罗不仅接受了基督的心思，更接受了祂整个内里的所是。
2　保罗内在的所是改变、重组、改造了。
3　他内在的所是被基督的心肠重构了─西三12。
三　那在基督里的真实，就是诚实、信实、可靠，也在保罗里面─林后十一10。
四　保罗对圣徒的爱，不是他的爱，乃是在基督里的爱，就是基督的爱；因此，保罗爱圣徒，不是凭他天然的爱，乃是凭基督的爱─林前十六24。
伍　保罗活在基督身体的实际里，乃是借着以基督对身体的感觉为自己的感觉─腓一8：
一　保罗是以基督耶稣的心肠为他自己的心肠来顾到基督的身体─8节。
二　我们都该像保罗一样，以元首基督的感觉为自己的感觉；对于我们活在基督身体的实际里，这是极其需要的─二1，西三12。
陆　我们要活基督，就必须在基督耶稣的心肠里生活─腓一21上，8：
一　保罗经历基督的心肠；他在基督的心肠里与基督是一，切切的想念圣徒─8节。
二　保罗没有在他天然的内在所是里生活，乃在基督的心肠里生活─西三12。
三　我们若要成为在基督里的人，就必须在祂的心肠里，在祂柔顺和细致的感觉里─约十五4上。
四　活基督乃是住在祂的心肠里，在其中享受祂作恩典─腓一7，四23。
柒　为着活在基督身体的实际里，我们需要穿上怜恤的心肠和恩慈─西三10～12：
一　怜恤是对另一个人的痛苦有深刻的认识，而且愿意减轻其痛苦─路六36：
1　虽然怜恤非常接近怜悯，但怜恤比怜悯更深、更细、更丰富─十33～34。
2　怜恤是最深刻的辞句，表明神对可怜光景中的人内里的情爱─诗一○三8，雅五11，林后一3。
3　怜恤的希腊原文乃指从一个情深的人心里所发出的内在感觉。
二　恩慈是一种仁慈的良善，出自怜悯和爱；神的恩典是在这样的恩慈中赐给我们的─多三4，弗二7：
1　那灵的果子其中的一项是恩慈─加五22。
2　乃是我们救主神的恩慈和爱拯救了我们，使我们与人有别─多三4，罗二4。
3　使徒保罗以恩慈作神的执事，并且他嘱咐我们要常留在神的恩慈中─林后六4，6，罗十一22。
4　在要来的诸世代─千年国时代和将来的永远─中，神要显示“祂在基督耶稣里，向我们所施恩慈中恩典超越的丰富”─弗二7。
5　爱是有恩慈（林前十三4），我们要以恩慈相待，心存慈怜，彼此饶恕，正如神在基督里饶恕了我们一样（弗四32）。─引用经文
捌　“你所喜爱的，是内里真实”─诗五一6上。

页首-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
LIVING IN THE REALITY OF THE BODY OF CHRIST BY LEARNING CHRIST AS THE REALITY IS IN JESUS
Message Seven
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus (1) Living in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus and Allowing Christ to Live in Our Inward Parts
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: Psa. 16:7; S. S. 5:14b; Phil. 1:8; Col. 3:12; Titus 3:4
I.　"All the churches will know that I am He who searches the inward parts and the hearts"—Rev. 2:23b.
II.　If we would live in the reality of the Body of Christ, we need to live in the inward parts of Christ Jesus and allow Christ to live in our inward parts—Phil. 1:8; Eph. 4:16.
III.　As a man, Christ had human inward parts with their various functions, and Christ's experiences in His inward parts were His experiences in His mind, emotion, will, soul, heart, and spirit, including His love, desire, feeling, thought, decision, motive, and intention—Luke 2:49; John 2:17; Matt. 26:39; Isa. 53:11-12; 42:4; Mark 2:8:
A.　The inward parts of the peace offering signify the tenderness, smallness, and preciousness of what Christ is in His inward being toward God for God's satisfaction—Lev. 3:3.
B.　Christ's inward parts instructed Him in the nights—Psa. 16:7b; Isa. 50:4:
1.　When God counseled Christ as a man, Christ's inward parts instructed Him through His contact with God—Psa. 16:7.
2.　The inward parts of Christ were one with God; this is the proper experience of a God-man—Phil. 1:8.
C.　"His belly is an ivory work, / Overlaid with sapphires" (S. S. 5:14b); Christ's inward parts (belly) are full of deep, tender feelings wrought through His sufferings (ivory work) under a clear heavenly vision (sapphire, cf. Exo. 24:10).
D.　Eating the passover lamb with its inward parts signifies taking Christ in His inward parts—12:9; Phil. 1:8.
IV.　Paul was a person who continually experienced Christ in His inward parts—v. 8; 2:5; 1 Cor. 2:16b; Rom. 8:6:
A.　Paul was one with Christ even in His inward parts—in His affection, tender mercy, and sympathy—Phil. 1:8.
B.　Paul did not keep his own inward parts but took Christ's inward parts as his—Eph. 3:17:
1.　Paul took not only Christ's mind but also His entire inward being.
2.　Paul's inner being was changed, rearranged, and remodeled.
3.　Paul's inward being was reconstituted with the inward parts of Christ—Col. 3:12.
C.　What was in Christ as truthfulness—as honesty, faithfulness, and trustworthiness— was also in Paul—2 Cor. 11:10.
D.　Paul's love for the saints was not his love but the love in Christ, which is Christ's love; thus, Paul loved the saints not by his natural love but by the love of Christ—1 Cor. 16:24.
V.　Paul lived in the reality of the Body of Christ by taking Christ's feeling for the Body as his own feeling—Phil. 1:8:
A.　Paul took the inward parts of Christ Jesus as his own inward parts for the Body of Christ—v. 8.
B.　Like Paul, we should take the feeling of Christ the Head as our own feeling; this is most necessary for our living in the reality of the Body of Christ—2:1; Col. 3:12.
VI.　To live Christ requires that we live in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—Phil. 1:21a, 8:
A.　Paul experienced the inward parts of Christ; he was one with Christ in His inward parts in longing after the saints—v. 8.
B.　Paul did not live a life in his natural inner being; he lived a life in the inward parts of Christ.
C.　If we would be those who are in Christ, we must be in His inward parts, in His tender and delicate feelings—John 15:4a.
D.　To live Christ is to abide in His inward parts and there to enjoy Him as grace—Phil. 1:7; 4:23.
VII.　For living in the reality of the Body of Christ, we need to put on inward parts of compassion and kindness—Col. 3:10-12:
A.　Compassion is a deep awareness of the suffering of another, coupled with the wish to relieve it—Luke 6:36:
1.　Although compassion is close to mercy, it is deeper, finer, and richer than mercy— 10:33-34.
2.　The word compassion is the deepest of words, showing the inward affection of God for man in his pitiful condition—Psa. 103:8; James 5:11; 2 Cor. 1:3.
3.　The Greek word for compassion refers to the inward feeling that originates in the heart of an affectionate person.
B.　Kindness is a benevolent goodness that issues out of mercy and love; it is in such kindness that the grace of God is given to us—Titus 3:4; Eph. 2:7:
1.　One item of the fruit of the Spirit is kindness—Gal. 5:22.
2.　It is the kindness and the love of our Savior God that saved us and made us different from others—Titus 3:4; Rom. 2:4.
3.　The apostle Paul was a minister of God in kindness, and he charges us to continue in the kindness of God—2 Cor. 6:4, 6; Rom. 11:22.
4.　In the ages to come—the ages of the millennium and eternity future—God will dis-play "the surpassing riches of His grace in kindness toward us in Christ Jesus"— Eph. 2:7.
5.　Love is kind (1 Cor. 13:4), and we need to be kind to one another, tenderhearted, forgiving one another, even as God in Christ also forgave us (Eph. 4:32).
VIII.　"You delight in truth in the inward parts"—Psa. 51:6a.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第七篇　活在基督耶稣的心肠里，而活在基督身体的实际里（一）活在基督耶稣的心肠里并让基督活在我们的心肠里
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus (1) Living in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus and Allowing Christ to Live in Our Inward Parts
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：诗十六7，歌五14下，腓一8，门7，20，西三12，多三4
壹　“叫众召会都知道，我是那察看人肺腑心肠的”─启二23中。
I.　"All the churches will know that I am He who searches the inward parts and the hearts"—Rev. 2:23b.
贰　我们若要活在基督身体的实际里，就需要活在基督耶稣的心肠里，并让基督活在我们的心肠里─腓一8，弗四16。
II.　If we would live in the reality of the Body of Christ, we need to live in the inward parts of Christ Jesus and allow Christ to live in our inward parts—Phil. 1:8; Eph. 4:16.
叁　基督成了人，就有人的心肠同其各种功用，基督在祂心肠里的经历，就是祂在祂心思、情感、意志、魂、心、灵里的经历，包括祂的爱好、愿望、感觉、思想、定意、存心和打算─路二49，约二17，太二六39，赛五三11～12，四二4，可二8：
III.　As a man, Christ had human inward parts with their various functions, and Christ's experiences in His inward parts were His experiences in His mind, emotion, will, soul, heart, and spirit, including His love, desire, feeling, thought, decision, motive, and intention—Luke 2:49; John 2:17; Matt. 26:39; Isa. 53:11-12; 42:4; Mark 2:8:
一　平安祭牲的内脏表征基督向着神之内里所是的柔顺、微小与宝贵，使神满足─利三3。
A.　The inward parts of the peace offering signify the tenderness, smallness, and preciousness of what Christ is in His inward being toward God for God's satisfaction—Lev. 3:3.
二　基督的心肠在夜间也警戒祂─诗十六7下，赛五十4：
B.　Christ's inward parts instructed Him in the nights—Psa. 16:7b; Isa. 50:4:
1　当神指教为人的基督时，基督借着与神接触，祂的心肠也警戒祂─诗十六7。
1.　When God counseled Christ as a man, Christ's inward parts instructed Him through His contact with God—Psa. 16:7.
2　基督的心肠与神是一；这是神人正确的经历─腓一8。
2.　The inward parts of Christ were one with God; this is the proper experience of a God-man—Phil. 1:8.
三　“他的肚腹如同象牙作的，外面包着蓝宝石”（歌五14下）；基督的心肠（肚腹）满了深刻、柔和的感觉，那是在明净的属天景象下（蓝宝石─参出二四10）借着受苦所作成的（象牙作的）。─引用经文
C.　"His belly is an ivory work, / Overlaid with sapphires" (S. S. 5:14b); Christ's inward parts (belly) are full of deep, tender feelings wrought through His sufferings (ivory work) under a clear heavenly vision (sapphire, cf. Exo. 24:10).
四　吃逾越节的羊羔，要带着内脏而吃，表征接受基督内里的诸部分─十二9，腓一8。
D.　Eating the passover lamb with its inward parts signifies taking Christ in His inward parts—12:9; Phil. 1:8.
肆　保罗是一个不断经历基督之心肠的人─腓一8，二5，林前二16下，罗八6：
IV.　Paul was a person who continually experienced Christ in His inward parts—v. 8; 2:5; 1 Cor. 2:16b; Rom. 8:6:
一　保罗甚至在基督的心肠，在祂的情感、柔细的怜悯以及同情里，与祂是一─腓一8。
A.　Paul was one with Christ even in His inward parts—in His affection, tender mercy, and sympathy—Phil. 1:8.
二　保罗没有持守自己的心肠，而是以基督的心肠为他的心肠─弗三17：
B.　Paul did not keep his own inward parts but took Christ's inward parts as his—Eph. 3:17:
1　保罗不仅接受了基督的心思，更接受了祂整个内里的所是。
1.　Paul took not only Christ's mind but also His entire inward being.
2　保罗内在的所是改变、重组、改造了。
2.　Paul's inner being was changed, rearranged, and remodeled.
3　他内在的所是被基督的心肠重构了─西三12。
3.　Paul's inward being was reconstituted with the inward parts of Christ—Col. 3:12.
三　那在基督里的真实，就是诚实、信实、可靠，也在保罗里面─林后十一10。
C.　What was in Christ as truthfulness—as honesty, faithfulness, and trustworthiness— was also in Paul—2 Cor. 11:10.
四　保罗对圣徒的爱，不是他的爱，乃是在基督里的爱，就是基督的爱；因此，保罗爱圣徒，不是凭他天然的爱，乃是凭基督的爱─林前十六24。
D.　Paul's love for the saints was not his love but the love in Christ, which is Christ's love; thus, Paul loved the saints not by his natural love but by the love of Christ—1 Cor. 16:24.
伍　保罗活在基督身体的实际里，乃是借着以基督对身体的感觉为自己的感觉─腓一8：
V.　Paul lived in the reality of the Body of Christ by taking Christ's feeling for the Body as his own feeling—Phil. 1:8:
一　保罗是以基督耶稣的心肠为他自己的心肠来顾到基督的身体─8节。
A.　Paul took the inward parts of Christ Jesus as his own inward parts for the Body of Christ—v. 8.
二　我们都该像保罗一样，以元首基督的感觉为自己的感觉；对于我们活在基督身体的实际里，这是极其需要的─二1，西三12。
B.　Like Paul, we should take the feeling of Christ the Head as our own feeling; this is most necessary for our living in the reality of the Body of Christ—2:1; Col. 3:12.
陆　我们要活基督，就必须在基督耶稣的心肠里生活─腓一21上，8：
VI.　To live Christ requires that we live in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—Phil. 1:21a, 8:
一　保罗经历基督的心肠；他在基督的心肠里与基督是一，切切的想念圣徒─8节。
A.　Paul experienced the inward parts of Christ; he was one with Christ in His inward parts in longing after the saints—v. 8.
二　保罗没有在他天然的内在所是里生活，乃在基督的心肠里生活─西三12。
B.　Paul did not live a life in his natural inner being; he lived a life in the inward parts of Christ.
三　我们若要成为在基督里的人，就必须在祂的心肠里，在祂柔顺和细致的感觉里─约十五4上。
C.　If we would be those who are in Christ, we must be in His inward parts, in His tender and delicate feelings—John 15:4a.
四　活基督乃是住在祂的心肠里，在其中享受祂作恩典─腓一7，四23。
D.　To live Christ is to abide in His inward parts and there to enjoy Him as grace—Phil. 1:7; 4:23.
柒　为着活在基督身体的实际里，我们需要穿上怜恤的心肠和恩慈─西三10～12：
VII.　For living in the reality of the Body of Christ, we need to put on inward parts of compassion and kindness—Col. 3:10-12:
一　怜恤是对另一个人的痛苦有深刻的认识，而且愿意减轻其痛苦─路六36：
A.　Compassion is a deep awareness of the suffering of another, coupled with the wish to relieve it—Luke 6:36:
1　虽然怜恤非常接近怜悯，但怜恤比怜悯更深、更细、更丰富─十33～34。
1.　Although compassion is close to mercy, it is deeper, finer, and richer than mercy— 10:33-34.
2　怜恤是最深刻的辞句，表明神对可怜光景中的人内里的情爱─诗一○三8，雅五11，林后一3。
2.　The word compassion is the deepest of words, showing the inward affection of God for man in his pitiful condition—Psa. 103:8; James 5:11; 2 Cor. 1:3.
3　怜恤的希腊原文乃指从一个情深的人心里所发出的内在感觉。
3.　The Greek word for compassion refers to the inward feeling that originates in the heart of an affectionate person.
二　恩慈是一种仁慈的良善，出自怜悯和爱；神的恩典是在这样的恩慈中赐给我们的─多三4，弗二7：
B.　Kindness is a benevolent goodness that issues out of mercy and love; it is in such kindness that the grace of God is given to us—Titus 3:4; Eph. 2:7:
1　那灵的果子其中的一项是恩慈─加五22。
1.　One item of the fruit of the Spirit is kindness—Gal. 5:22.
2　乃是我们救主神的恩慈和爱拯救了我们，使我们与人有别─多三4，罗二4。
2.　It is the kindness and the love of our Savior God that saved us and made us different from others—Titus 3:4; Rom. 2:4.
3　使徒保罗以恩慈作神的执事，并且他嘱咐我们要常留在神的恩慈中─林后六4，6，罗十一22。
3.　The apostle Paul was a minister of God in kindness, and he charges us to continue in the kindness of God—2 Cor. 6:4, 6; Rom. 11:22.
4　在要来的诸世代─千年国时代和将来的永远─中，神要显示“祂在基督耶稣里，向我们所施恩慈中恩典超越的丰富”─弗二7。
4.　In the ages to come—the ages of the millennium and eternity future—God will dis-play "the surpassing riches of His grace in kindness toward us in Christ Jesus"— Eph. 2:7.
5　爱是有恩慈（林前十三4），我们要以恩慈相待，心存慈怜，彼此饶恕，正如神在基督里饶恕了我们一样（弗四32）。─引用经文
5.　Love is kind (1 Cor. 13:4), and we need to be kind to one another, tenderhearted, forgiving one another, even as God in Christ also forgave us (Eph. 4:32).
捌　“你所喜爱的，是内里真实”─诗五一6上。
VIII.　"You delight in truth in the inward parts"—Psa. 51:6a.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第八篇　活在基督耶稣的心肠里，而活在基督身体的实际里（二）有基督身体的感觉并在基督耶稣的心肠里实行召会生活，而活在基督的身体里
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：林前十二26～27，罗十二4～5，15，门7，12～16，20
壹　我们越活在基督耶稣的心肠里，我们的身体感会越重，我们对基督身体的感觉也会越强─林前十二26～27，罗十二15：
一　我们要过身体生活，就需要对基督的身体有感觉─4～5，15节。
二　基督身体的感觉，就是基督的生命在我们里面所有的感觉─西三4，15，罗八2，6，10～11，十二4～5：
1　这个感觉是出乎神的灵，也是出乎我们灵里神的生命─八2，9～10。
2　我们若操练这个感觉，这个感觉会叫我们感觉到与身体有关的事，这感觉也会成为身体的感觉─十二15，林后十一28～29。
3　我们若是有身体的感觉，知觉，当人遭遇为难或蒙福时，我们都会感同身受，同样的感到为难，同样的感到蒙福─林前十二26～27。
三　基督身体的感觉来自与基督生机的联结、对基督的享受、以及活在基督耶稣的心肠里─罗十二4～5，西二16～19，腓一8：
1　我们可以借着活在与基督生机的联结里，来培养基督身体的感觉─罗十二4～5：
a　罗马十二章是由生机的联结、联结的生命这个角度来论到基督的身体，这个生命不但把我们与基督联结在一起，也把我们与基督所有的肢体联结在一起。
b　我们在基督里是一个身体，与祂有生机的联结；这联结使我们与基督是一，也与祂身体上所有其他的肢体是一─4～5节。
2　我们可以借着享受包罗万有的基督，就是身体的头，来培养基督身体的感觉─西二16～19：
a　我们所享受这位宝贵、包罗万有的基督，乃是身体的头─林前十3～4，约二十22，西一18，二19。
b　我们所享受的基督乃是头，祂使我们对身体有感觉；因此，享受基督和持定祂作元首的结果，乃是我们有基督身体的感觉─16～19节。
3　我们可以借着活在基督耶稣的心肠里，来培养身体的感觉─腓一8，西三10～12，15。
贰　在保罗给腊利门的书信里有一幅图昼，描绘在基督耶稣的心肠里生活的召会生活─7，10～16，20节：
一　心肠，表征内在的情爱、慈心、怜恤─腓一8，二1，西三12。
二　保罗内在的情爱和怜恤，随同欧尼西母到腓利门那里去─门12。
三　“弟兄阿，是的，愿我在主里从你得着益处，愿你使我的心肠在基督里得舒畅”─20节：
1　腓利门二十节揭示，基督是使信徒心肠得舒畅的范围和元素。
2　得舒畅，意“得抚慰”、“感畅快”。
3　腓利门既然使众圣徒的心肠得了舒畅（7），现今保罗要求他在主里也这样待他。─引用经文
4　保罗所说在主里的益处，是指他的心肠在基督里得舒畅：
a　腓利门无法在自己里面或凭着自己，叫保罗的心肠得舒畅，而必须在主里，在基督里。
b　保罗向腓利门所寻求的益处─使他的心肠得舒畅─乃是来自于主。
c　惟有在基督里，我们的心肠才能因同作信徒者得舒畅；这就是经历并享受基督作为使信徒心肠得舒畅的范围和元素。
5　借着活在基督耶稣的心肠里，并借着舒畅一我们的心肠在基督里借着别人得舒畅，以及信徒的心肠借着我们得舒畅─我们可以有甜美愉悦的召会生活。
叁　腓利门书该看作歌罗西四章的延续，并且视为在新人里一切社会阶级如何该放在一边的例证─门1～2，10～19：
一　信徒中间社会阶级和身分的分别已被废除，因为信徒已由作他们生命之包罗万有的基督所构成─西三4。
二　在腓利门书中，保罗给众召会一个例证，就是奴仆和主人如何被基督所重新构成；结果，他们都是新人的一部分，并且在新人里有平等的身分─西三10～11。
三　在神经纶的实行里，消除一切社会阶级和种族、国籍之间的不同，乃是要紧的─10～11节：
1　在新人里，基于肤色的分别已被废掉；保罗厉害的教导这点，我们必须将其视为对真理之完全认识的一部分─提前二4，提后二25，多一1。
2　我们若看见信徒在新人里有平等的身分，我们中间就不会有关于社会阶级、国籍、或种族的难处─林前十二13，加三28，西三10～11。
四　腓利门书的主题是在新人里信徒身分平等的例证─弗二15，四24：
1　欧尼西母和腓利门的事例，说明所有的信徒在新人里有平等的身分─门1～2，10～19。
2　因着神圣的出生，以及凭着神圣生命而有的生活，所有在基督里的信徒，在一个新人中都有平等的身分─弗四24，西三10。

页首-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
LIVING IN THE REALITY OF THE BODY OF CHRIST BY LEARNING CHRIST AS THE REALITY IS IN JESUS
Message Eight
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus (2) Living in the Body of Christ by Being Conscious of the Body and Practicing a Church Life in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: 1 Cor. 12:26-27; Rom. 12:4-5, 15; Philem. 7, 12-16, 20
I.　The more we live in the inward parts of Christ Jesus, the greater will be our consciousness of the Body of Christ and the stronger will be our feeling for the Body of Christ—1 Cor. 12:26-27; Rom. 12:15:
A.　In order to live the Body life, we need to be conscious of the Body of Christ—vv. 4-5, 15.
B.　The consciousness of the Body of Christ is the sense of Christ's life within us—Col. 3:4, 15; Rom. 8:2, 6, 10-11; 12:4-5:
1.　This sense originates from the Spirit of God and from God's life in our spirit—8:2, 9-10.
2.　If we exercise this sense, it will cause us to become conscious of matters related to the Body, and this sense will become the consciousness of the Body—12:15; 2 Cor. 11:28-29.
3.　If we have the sense, the consciousness, of the Body, when others suffer or are blessed, we will identify with them and feel the same hardship or blessing—1 Cor. 12:26-27.
C.　The consciousness of the Body of Christ comes from the organic union with Christ, the enjoyment of Christ, and the living in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—Rom. 12:4-5; Col. 2:16-19; Phil. 1:8:
1.　We may cultivate the consciousness of the Body by living in the organic union with Christ—Rom. 12:4-5:
a.　Romans 12 speaks of the Body from the angle of the organic union, from a life that unites us not only with Christ but with all the other members of Christ.
b.　We are one Body in Christ, having an organic union with Him; this union makes us one with Christ and with all the other members of the Body—vv. 4-5.
2.　We may cultivate the consciousness of the Body by enjoying the all-inclusive Christ, who is the Head of the Body—Col. 2:16-19:
a.　The precious, all-inclusive Christ whom we enjoy is the Head of the Body— 1 Cor. 10:3-4; John 20:22; Col. 1:18; 2:19.
b.　The Christ whom we enjoy is the Head who causes us to be conscious of the Body; therefore, the issue of enjoying Christ and holding Him as the Head is that we have the consciousness of the Body of Christ—vv. 16-19.
3.　We may cultivate the consciousness of the Body by living in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—Phil. 1:8; Col. 3:10-12, 15.
II.　In Paul's Epistle to Philemon we have a picture of the church life lived in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—vv. 7, 10-16, 20:
A.　The inward parts signify inward affection, tenderheartedness, and compassions—Phil. 1:8; 2:1; Col. 3:12.
B.　Paul's inward affection and compassions went with Onesimus to Philemon—Philem. 12.
C.　"Brother, may I have profit from you in the Lord; refresh my inward parts in Christ"— v. 20:
1.　In Philemon 20 Christ is unveiled as the sphere and element for the refreshing of the believers' inward parts.
2.　The word refresh means "soothe," or "cheer."
3.　Since Philemon had refreshed the inward parts of the saints (v. 7), Paul now asked him to do the same for him in the Lord.
4.　The profit in the Lord that Paul speaks of refers to being refreshed in his inward parts in Christ:
a.　The refreshing of Paul's inward parts could not have been done in or by Philemon himself but only in the Lord and in Christ.
b.　The profit—being refreshed in his inward parts—that Paul sought from Philemon comes out of the Lord.
c.　It is only in Christ that we can be refreshed in our inward parts by fellow believers; this is to experience and enjoy Christ as the sphere and element for the refreshing of the believers' inward parts.
5.　By living in the inward parts of Christ Jesus and by refreshing—having our inward parts refreshed by others in Christ and the believers' inward parts being refreshed through us—we may have a sweet and pleasant church life.
III.　The Epistle to Philemon should be regarded as a continuation of Colossians 4 and considered an illustration of how in the one new man all social rank is put aside— Philem. 1-2, 10-19:
A.　The distinction of social rank and status among the believers has been nullified because the believers have been constituted with the all-inclusive Christ, who is their life—Col. 3:4.
B.　In the Epistle to Philemon Paul gives the churches an illustration of how slaves and masters have been reconstituted with Christ; as a result, they are all part of the new man and have an equal status in the new man—Col. 3:10-11.
C.　In the practice of the economy of God, it is crucial that all social ranks and differences among races and nations are swallowed up—vv. 10-11:
1.　In the new man distinctions on the basis of color have been nullified; Paul strongly taught this, and we must consider it part of the full knowledge of the truth—1 Tim. 2:4; 2 Tim. 2:25; Titus 1:1.
2.　If we see that the believers have an equal status in the new man, there will be no problems among us concerning social rank, nationality, or race—1 Cor. 12:13; Gal. 3:28; Col. 3:10-11.
D.　The subject of the book of Philemon is an illustration of the believers' equal status in the new man—Eph. 2:15; 4:24:
1.　The case of Onesimus and Philemon illustrates that in the new man all the believers have an equal status—Philem. 1-2, 10-19.
2.　Because of the divine birth and a living by the divine life, all the believers in Christ have equal status in the one new man—Eph. 4:24; Col. 3:10.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第八篇　活在基督耶稣的心肠里，而活在基督身体的实际里（二）有基督身体的感觉并在基督耶稣的心肠里实行召会生活，而活在基督的身体里
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus (2) Living in the Body of Christ by Being Conscious of the Body and Practicing a Church Life in the Inward Parts of Christ Jesus
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：林前十二26～27，罗十二4～5，15，门7，12～16，20
壹　我们越活在基督耶稣的心肠里，我们的身体感会越重，我们对基督身体的感觉也会越强─林前十二26～27，罗十二15：
I.　The more we live in the inward parts of Christ Jesus, the greater will be our consciousness of the Body of Christ and the stronger will be our feeling for the Body of Christ—1 Cor. 12:26-27; Rom. 12:15:
一　我们要过身体生活，就需要对基督的身体有感觉─4～5，15节。
A.　In order to live the Body life, we need to be conscious of the Body of Christ—vv. 4-5, 15.
二　基督身体的感觉，就是基督的生命在我们里面所有的感觉─西三4，15，罗八2，6，10～11，十二4～5：
B.　The consciousness of the Body of Christ is the sense of Christ's life within us—Col. 3:4, 15; Rom. 8:2, 6, 10-11; 12:4-5:
1　这个感觉是出乎神的灵，也是出乎我们灵里神的生命─八2，9～10。
1.　This sense originates from the Spirit of God and from God's life in our spirit—8:2, 9-10.
2　我们若操练这个感觉，这个感觉会叫我们感觉到与身体有关的事，这感觉也会成为身体的感觉─十二15，林后十一28～29。
2.　If we exercise this sense, it will cause us to become conscious of matters related to the Body, and this sense will become the consciousness of the Body—12:15; 2 Cor. 11:28-29.
3　我们若是有身体的感觉，知觉，当人遭遇为难或蒙福时，我们都会感同身受，同样的感到为难，同样的感到蒙福─林前十二26～27。
3.　If we have the sense, the consciousness, of the Body, when others suffer or are blessed, we will identify with them and feel the same hardship or blessing—1 Cor. 12:26-27.
三　基督身体的感觉来自与基督生机的联结、对基督的享受、以及活在基督耶稣的心肠里─罗十二4～5，西二16～19，腓一8：
C.　The consciousness of the Body of Christ comes from the organic union with Christ, the enjoyment of Christ, and the living in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—Rom. 12:4-5; Col. 2:16-19; Phil. 1:8:
1　我们可以借着活在与基督生机的联结里，来培养基督身体的感觉─罗十二4～5：
1.　We may cultivate the consciousness of the Body by living in the organic union with Christ—Rom. 12:4-5:
a　罗马十二章是由生机的联结、联结的生命这个角度来论到基督的身体，这个生命不但把我们与基督联结在一起，也把我们与基督所有的肢体联结在一起。
a.　Romans 12 speaks of the Body from the angle of the organic union, from a life that unites us not only with Christ but with all the other members of Christ.
b　我们在基督里是一个身体，与祂有生机的联结；这联结使我们与基督是一，也与祂身体上所有其他的肢体是一─4～5节。
b.　We are one Body in Christ, having an organic union with Him; this union makes us one with Christ and with all the other members of the Body—vv. 4-5.
2　我们可以借着享受包罗万有的基督，就是身体的头，来培养基督身体的感觉─西二16～19：
2.　We may cultivate the consciousness of the Body by enjoying the all-inclusive Christ, who is the Head of the Body—Col. 2:16-19:
a　我们所享受这位宝贵、包罗万有的基督，乃是身体的头─林前十3～4，约二十22，西一18，二19。
a.　The precious, all-inclusive Christ whom we enjoy is the Head of the Body— 1 Cor. 10:3-4; John 20:22; Col. 1:18; 2:19.
b　我们所享受的基督乃是头，祂使我们对身体有感觉；因此，享受基督和持定祂作元首的结果，乃是我们有基督身体的感觉─16～19节。
b.　The Christ whom we enjoy is the Head who causes us to be conscious of the Body; therefore, the issue of enjoying Christ and holding Him as the Head is that we have the consciousness of the Body of Christ—vv. 16-19.
3　我们可以借着活在基督耶稣的心肠里，来培养身体的感觉─腓一8，西三10～12，15。
3.　We may cultivate the consciousness of the Body by living in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—Phil. 1:8; Col. 3:10-12, 15.
贰　在保罗给腊利门的书信里有一幅图昼，描绘在基督耶稣的心肠里生活的召会生活─7，10～16，20节：
II.　In Paul's Epistle to Philemon we have a picture of the church life lived in the inward parts of Christ Jesus—vv. 7, 10-16, 20:
一　心肠，表征内在的情爱、慈心、怜恤─腓一8，二1，西三12。
A.　The inward parts signify inward affection, tenderheartedness, and compassions—Phil. 1:8; 2:1; Col. 3:12.
二　保罗内在的情爱和怜恤，随同欧尼西母到腓利门那里去─门12。
B.　Paul's inward affection and compassions went with Onesimus to Philemon—Philem. 12.
三　“弟兄阿，是的，愿我在主里从你得着益处，愿你使我的心肠在基督里得舒畅”─20节：
C.　"Brother, may I have profit from you in the Lord; refresh my inward parts in Christ"— v. 20:
1　腓利门二十节揭示，基督是使信徒心肠得舒畅的范围和元素。
1.　In Philemon 20 Christ is unveiled as the sphere and element for the refreshing of the believers' inward parts.
2　得舒畅，意“得抚慰”、“感畅快”。
2.　The word refresh means "soothe," or "cheer."
3　腓利门既然使众圣徒的心肠得了舒畅（7），现今保罗要求他在主里也这样待他。─引用经文
3.　Since Philemon had refreshed the inward parts of the saints (v. 7), Paul now asked him to do the same for him in the Lord.
4　保罗所说在主里的益处，是指他的心肠在基督里得舒畅：
4.　The profit in the Lord that Paul speaks of refers to being refreshed in his inward parts in Christ:
a　腓利门无法在自己里面或凭着自己，叫保罗的心肠得舒畅，而必须在主里，在基督里。
a.　The refreshing of Paul's inward parts could not have been done in or by Philemon himself but only in the Lord and in Christ.
b　保罗向腓利门所寻求的益处─使他的心肠得舒畅─乃是来自于主。
b.　The profit—being refreshed in his inward parts—that Paul sought from Philemon comes out of the Lord.
c　惟有在基督里，我们的心肠才能因同作信徒者得舒畅；这就是经历并享受基督作为使信徒心肠得舒畅的范围和元素。
c.　It is only in Christ that we can be refreshed in our inward parts by fellow believers; this is to experience and enjoy Christ as the sphere and element for the refreshing of the believers' inward parts.
5　借着活在基督耶稣的心肠里，并借着舒畅一我们的心肠在基督里借着别人得舒畅，以及信徒的心肠借着我们得舒畅─我们可以有甜美愉悦的召会生活。
5.　By living in the inward parts of Christ Jesus and by refreshing—having our inward parts refreshed by others in Christ and the believers' inward parts being refreshed through us—we may have a sweet and pleasant church life.
叁　腓利门书该看作歌罗西四章的延续，并且视为在新人里一切社会阶级如何该放在一边的例证─门1～2，10～19：
III.　The Epistle to Philemon should be regarded as a continuation of Colossians 4 and considered an illustration of how in the one new man all social rank is put aside— Philem. 1-2, 10-19:
一　信徒中间社会阶级和身分的分别已被废除，因为信徒已由作他们生命之包罗万有的基督所构成─西三4。
A.　The distinction of social rank and status among the believers has been nullified because the believers have been constituted with the all-inclusive Christ, who is their life—Col. 3:4.
二　在腓利门书中，保罗给众召会一个例证，就是奴仆和主人如何被基督所重新构成；结果，他们都是新人的一部分，并且在新人里有平等的身分─西三10～11。
B.　In the Epistle to Philemon Paul gives the churches an illustration of how slaves and masters have been reconstituted with Christ; as a result, they are all part of the new man and have an equal status in the new man—Col. 3:10-11.
三　在神经纶的实行里，消除一切社会阶级和种族、国籍之间的不同，乃是要紧的─10～11节：
C.　In the practice of the economy of God, it is crucial that all social ranks and differences among races and nations are swallowed up—vv. 10-11:
1　在新人里，基于肤色的分别已被废掉；保罗厉害的教导这点，我们必须将其视为对真理之完全认识的一部分─提前二4，提后二25，多一1。
1.　In the new man distinctions on the basis of color have been nullified; Paul strongly taught this, and we must consider it part of the full knowledge of the truth—1 Tim. 2:4; 2 Tim. 2:25; Titus 1:1.
2　我们若看见信徒在新人里有平等的身分，我们中间就不会有关于社会阶级、国籍、或种族的难处─林前十二13，加三28，西三10～11。
2.　If we see that the believers have an equal status in the new man, there will be no problems among us concerning social rank, nationality, or race—1 Cor. 12:13; Gal. 3:28; Col. 3:10-11.
四　腓利门书的主题是在新人里信徒身分平等的例证─弗二15，四24：
D.　The subject of the book of Philemon is an illustration of the believers' equal status in the new man—Eph. 2:15; 4:24:
1　欧尼西母和腓利门的事例，说明所有的信徒在新人里有平等的身分─门1～2，10～19。
1.　The case of Onesimus and Philemon illustrates that in the new man all the believers have an equal status—Philem. 1-2, 10-19.
2　因着神圣的出生，以及凭着神圣生命而有的生活，所有在基督里的信徒，在一个新人中都有平等的身分─弗四24，西三10。
2.　Because of the divine birth and a living by the divine life, all the believers in Christ have equal status in the one new man—Eph. 4:24; Col. 3:10.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第九篇　活神是爱的生活，而活在基督身体的实际里
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：林前八1下，十二31下，十三1，4～8，13，十四1，3，4下，约二一15～17，启三7～22
壹　在我们的基督徒生活和召会生活中，爱必须有效能─林前十二31下，十三4～8，13：
一　我们必须是被基督的爱冲没并冲激的人；神圣的爱该像大水澎湃冲向我们，迫使我们情不自禁的向祂活着并爱祂到极点─林后五14。
二　我们必须保守自己在神的爱中，并被基督的爱困迫，以至于为弟兄舍命─犹19～21，林后五14，彼前一22，约壹三14～16，四7～21。
三　我们要爱主到极点，就必须渴望并寻求一生一世住在神的殿中，瞻仰祂的荣美（可爱、可悦、可喜），在神的殿里求问神；求问神就是在我们日常生活中凡事问问神─诗二七4。
四　为着建造召会作基督生机的身体，在我们的所是和所作上，爱乃是极超越的路─林前十二31下，十三1，4～8，13：
1　保罗在林前十三章所描述的爱，乃是神圣生命的彰显（4～8上）；不仅如此，爱乃是那灵的果子，这指明爱的本质必须是那灵（加五22）；我们若没有爱，我们的说话就如同鸣的锣、响的钹，发出声音却没有生命（林前十三1，十四1，3，4下，12，31，林后三6）。─引用经文
2　我们在爱别人的事上，应当像神一样，一无分别的爱人（太五43～48）；基督借着钉十字架而拯救的第一个人，不是一个绅士，而是一个罪犯，一个判处死刑的强盗；这是非常有意义的（二七38，路二三42～43）。─引用经文
3　当生命之灵的律作为爱的律在我们里面得以发动，我们就自动并自然的成为牧人，有我们父神爱和赦免的心，并我们救主基督牧养和寻找的灵─罗八2，加六2～3，约二一15～17，路十五3～7。
4　我们在主里的劳苦乃是爱心的劳苦（林前十五58，帖前一3）；在其中我们“扶助软弱的人”（徒二十35）并“扶持软弱的人”（帖前五14）；“软弱的人”指那些在灵、魂、体方面软弱，或是在信心上软弱的人（罗十四1，十五1）。─引用经文
五　“知识是叫人自高自大，惟有爱建造人”；我们可能听了职事的信息，只得了一些知识，就自高自大─林前八1下，参林后三6。
贰　主现今并终极恢复之现有的真理，乃是借着我们拣选走非拉铁非的路，将我们带进新的复兴，以转移时代；惟有恢复的召会，就是在非拉铁非的召会所表征之弟兄相爱的召会，才能成就神永远的定旨，并满足祂心头的愿望─启一1～3，三7～13，诗歌六四〇首：
一　在非拉铁非的得胜者（7～13），其特征是他们渴望达到神经纶之神圣启示的最高峰─这最高峰就是神成为人，为要使人在生命和性情上，但不在神格上，成为神，使基督的身体得以产生，基督的新妇得以预备好，新耶路撒冷得以终极完成：
1　虽然普遍说来，在亚西亚的众召会离弃了使徒保罗的职事（提后一15），但有一个召会是独特的，非常受主称赞─在非拉铁非的召会；主非常称赞他们，甚至珍赏他们，因为他们遵守主的话，那就是说，他们没有离弃使徒保罗关于神经纶之健康教训的话语，就是神圣启示的最高峰（启三8，提前一3～4，六3）。─引用经文
2　那些在非拉铁非的人，借着祷读并默想神的话，将祂的话珍藏在心里（弗六17～18，诗一一九11，15），“对神〔是〕富足的”（路十二21）；他们向神的话举手，指明他们热诚欢乐的接受它，并对它说，阿们（诗一一九48，尼八5～6）。─引用经文
3　得胜者在殿中作柱子，意思就是他们要在三一神里作柱子，因为殿就是“主神全能者和羔羊”；神建造到他们里面，使他们成为宝贵的石头，他们也建造到神里面，使他们成为在神里面的石柱，他们就与神合并，作神与人相互的住处─启三12上，二一22，3，诗九十1，约十四23，参王上七17。
4　将神的名，新耶路撒冷的名，并主的新名，写在得胜者上面，指明神的所是、新耶路撒冷的性质并主的人位，全都作到他们里面，使他们有三一神为标示，作他们的“名牌”，并使他们在生命和性情上成为神，但无分于神格─启三12下，二4下。
二　在非拉铁非的得胜者，其特征是他们借着享受基督的丰富作他们内住的宝贝，而竭力进入神人的生活─三7，赛二二15，20～24：
1　在以赛亚二十二章，神解雇舍伯那，就是王家里的家宰（15～19），而用预表包罗万有之基督的以利亚敬顶替；基督是神家的管家，乃是肩头上放着神家之钥匙的一位（20～25，启三7～8）；基督有支配神宝库之门的钥匙，在这宝库中，有神在基督里的丰富作我们的享受（帖前五16～19，参结一22，26）：─引用经文
a　真正的召会生活，乃是众圣徒都被解雇，而被基督顶替，使基督在召会中成为一切的生活；我们众人都是“舍伯那”，该被基督这真以利亚敬除去并顶替，使我们成为祂这位神奥秘与神诸般恩典之管家的复制─西三10～11，林前四1，彼前四10。
b　因着我们已经与基督联合，基督也使祂自己与我们联合，与我们联结，所以当祂死在十字架上时，我们就与祂同死，且被了结；如今在我们与基督生机的联结中，祂活在我们里面，与我们同活，借着我们并经过我们而活，因而顶替了我们─罗六6，加二20，罗八16，林前六17。
2　主用大卫的钥匙开启扩展祂恢复的门，对我们是客观的，但基督也用大卫的钥匙主观的开启我们里面之人的门，使我们变化并建造成为神的殿，作柱子，有神的名，新耶路撒冷的名，并主的新名─启二17，三12，参二一22：
a　“我神的名”指明柱子是神；“我神城的名”指明柱子是新耶路撒冷；“我的新名”指明柱子是具有新意义的基督；得胜者作为柱子，成为神（在生命和性情上，但无分于神格）、成为新耶路撒冷的构成分子、并成为在新的经历意义上的基督─三12。
b　新耶路撒冷乃是新的基督；我们作为神的扩大和扩展，乃是具有新意义的基督，就是新耶路撒冷；新的基督与祂在四福音书里不一样；新妇作为新郎的扩增，乃是新耶路撒冷，包括所有由神重生的人─约三29～30，启二一9～10。
c　我们要被建造到神里面，成为新耶路撒冷的构成成分，并成为新的基督的一部分，就人说是不可能的，但我们里面生命之灵的律包含一个元素，能对付不可能─罗八2，路十八27，参创二八12～19，约一51。
三　在非拉铁非的得胜者，其特征是弟兄相爱；在他们中间，爱是有效能的，以致他们按着神牧养人（彼前五2），以令人愉快之神的同在顾惜人，并以神经纶健康的教训喂养人（弗四11，五29，徒二十28）：─引用经文
1　召会生活乃是弟兄相爱的生活（约壹四7～8，约贰5～6，约十五12，17，启三7，弗五2，参犹12上），并且身体在爱里把自己建造起来（弗四16）。─引用经文
2　在非拉铁非的得胜者站在一的真正立场上，并保守自己在神的爱里，爱主并爱所有的弟兄们─启三7上，参二4，7，犹19～21，林后五14，约十二3，路七47，约壹三14～16，诗一三三。
3　在非拉铁非的得胜者持守主在祂独一新约职事里的话（启三8），这话将他们带进对作他们的生命和一切之主耶稣基督自己这宝贵人位的真实珍赏、爱和享受里（林后十一2～3）。─引用经文
4　我们要将生命供应给人，并维持我们的得胜，以建造召会，就必须从我们对主的爱和对弟兄们的爱，涌流出复兴的生活并在牧养上的劳苦─箴四18，约二一15～17。
四　我们若要持续走非拉铁非的路，就必须蒙拯救脱离老底嘉的路，也就是堕落并走了样的非拉铁非─启三14～22：
1　老底嘉记得自己已往的故事，但是已往的生命没有了；我们必须一直记住，重要的乃是神现今的同在─出三三14，林后二10。
2　老底嘉，就是说起来样样都知道，事实上没有一样是热切的；说起来样样都有，但是没有一样是能够把命拚上的；记得已往时候的光荣，却忘记了今天在神面前的光景；已往是非拉铁非，今天是老底嘉，满了不冷不热和属灵的骄傲─启三15～17。
3　我们如果要继续在非拉铁非的道路上，就得在神面前谦卑自己，并付代价得着更多三一神作金子、白衣和眼药；这样，我们就能与主这位在我们里面领头的得胜者是一，好在千年国里与祂一同坐在祂的宝座上─18，21节。

页首-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
LIVING IN THE REALITY OF THE BODY OF CHRIST BY LEARNING CHRIST AS THE REALITY IS IN JESUS
Message Nine
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living a Life of God as Love
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: 1 Cor. 8:1b; 12:31b; 13:1, 4-8, 13; 14:1, 3, 4b; John 21:15-17; Rev. 3:7-22
I.　In our Christian life and church life, love must prevail—1 Cor. 12:31b; 13:4-8, 13:
A.　We must be persons who are flooded with and carried away by the love of Christ; the divine love should be like the rushing tide of great waters toward us, impelling us to live to Him and love Him to the uttermost beyond our own control—2 Cor. 5:14.
B.　We must keep ourselves in the love of God and be constrained by the love of Christ to lay down our lives on behalf of the brothers—Jude 19-21; 2 Cor. 5:14; 1 Pet. 1:22; 1 John 3:14-16; 4:7-21.
C.　In order to love the Lord to the uttermost, we need to be those who desire and seek to dwell in the house of God all the days of our life, to behold His beauty (loveliness, pleasantness, delightfulness), and to inquire of God in His temple; to inquire of God is to check with God about everything in our daily life—Psa. 27:4.
D.　Love is the most excellent way for us to be anything or do anything for the building up of the church as the organic Body of Christ—1 Cor. 12:31b; 13:1, 4-8, 13:
1.　The love described by Paul in 1 Corinthians 13 is the expression of the divine life (vv. 4-8a); furthermore, the fact that love is the fruit of the Spirit indicates that the substance of love must be the Spirit (Gal. 5:22); if we do not have love, our speaking is like that of sounding brass and a clanging cymbal, which give sounds without life (1 Cor. 13:1; 14:1, 3, 4b, 12, 31; 2 Cor. 3:6).
2.　We should be like God in our love for others, loving people without any discrimination (Matt. 5:43-48); the first one saved by Christ through His crucifixion was not a gentleman but a criminal, a robber, sentenced to death; this is very meaningful (27:38; Luke 23:42-43).
3.　When the law of the Spirit of life as the law of love is activated within us, we automatically and spontaneously will be shepherds who have the loving and forgiving heart of our Father God and the shepherding and seeking spirit of our Savior Christ— Rom. 8:2; Gal. 6:2-3; John 21:15-17; Luke 15:3-7.
4.　Our labor in the Lord is a labor of love (1 Cor. 15:58; 1 Thes. 1:3) in which we "support the weak" (Acts 20:35) and "sustain the weak" (1 Thes. 5:14); the weak refers to those who are weak either in their spirit, soul, or body, or are weak in faith (Rom. 14:1; 15:1).
E.　"Knowledge puffs up, but love builds up"; we may listen to the messages of the ministry and become puffed up with mere knowledge—1 Cor. 8:1b; cf. 2 Cor. 3:6.
II.　The present truth of the Lord's up-to-date and ultimate recovery is to bring us into a new revival to turn the age by our choosing to take the way of Philadelphia; only the recovered church, the church of brotherly love, signified by the church in Philadelphia, can fulfill God's eternal purpose and satisfy His heart's desire— Rev. 1:1-3; 3:7-13; Hymns, #880:
A.　The characteristic of the overcomers in Philadelphia (vv. 7-13) is their aspiration to arrive at the highest peak of the divine revelation of God's economy—this highest peak is God becoming man to make man God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead so that the Body of Christ can be produced, the bride can be prepared, and the New Jerusalem can be consummated:
1.　Even though the churches in Asia, in a general sense, had turned away from the apostle Paul's ministry (2 Tim. 1:15), one church was unique and was highly appraised by the Lord—the church in Philadelphia; the Lord highly appraised them and even appreciated them because they kept His word, which means that they did not turn away from the word of the apostle Paul's healthy teaching of God's economy, the highest peak of the divine revelation (Rev. 3:8; 1 Tim. 1:3-4; 6:3).
2.　Those in Philadelphia are "rich toward God" (Luke 12:21) by pray-reading and musing upon His word to treasure up His word in their heart (Eph. 6:17-18; Psa. 119:11, 15); they lift up their hands unto the word of God, indicating that they receive it warmly and gladly and that they say Amen to it (v. 48; Neh. 8:5-6).
3.　For the overcomers to be pillars in the temple means that they will be pillars in the Triune God, for the temple is "the Lord God the Almighty and the Lamb"; God is built into them to make them precious stones, and they are built into God to make them pillars of stone in God for their incorporation with God as the mutual abode of God and man—Rev. 3:12a; 21:22, 3; Psa. 90:1; John 14:23; cf. 1 Kings 7:17.
4.　That the name of God, the name of the New Jerusalem, and the Lord's new name are written upon the overcomers indicates that what God is, the nature of the New Jerusalem, and the person of the Lord have all been wrought into them, labeling them with the Triune God as their "name badge" and making them God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead—Rev. 3:12b; 22:4b.
B.　The characteristic of the overcomers in Philadelphia is their endeavoring to enter into the God-man living by enjoying the riches of Christ as their indwelling treasure—Eph. 3:8; 2 Cor. 4:7:
1.　In Isaiah 22 God fired Shebna, a steward in the house of the king (vv. 15-19), and replaced him with Eliakim, a type of the all-inclusive Christ as the Steward in God's house, the One upon whose shoulder the key of the house of God is set (vv. 20-25; Rev. 3:7-8); Christ has the key to control the door of God's treasury, in which are the riches of God in Christ for our enjoyment (1 Thes. 5:16-19; cf. Ezek. 1:22, 26):
a.　The real church life is a life in which all the saints are fired and replaced with Christ, making Christ everything in the church; all of us are Shebnas, who should be removed and replaced by Christ as the real Eliakim to make us His duplication as stewards of the mysteries of God and the varied grace of God— Col. 3:10-11; 1 Cor. 4:1; 1 Pet. 4:10.
b.　Because we have been joined to Christ, and Christ joined Himself to us, uniting Himself with us, when He died on the cross, we died with Him and were terminated; now in our organic union with Christ, He replaces us by living in us, with us, by us, and through us—Rom. 6:6; Gal. 2:20; Rom. 8:16; 1 Cor. 6:17.
2.　The Lord's using the key of David to open the door for the spread of His recovery is objective to us, but Christ is also using the key of David to subjectively open the door in our inner being for us to be transformed and built into the house of God as a pillar with the name of God, the name of the New Jerusalem, and the new name of the Lord—Rev. 2:17; 3:12; cf. 21:22:
a.　The name of My God indicates that the pillar is God; the name of the city of My God indicates that the pillar is the New Jerusalem; and My new name indicates that the pillar is Christ in a new significance; the overcomer as a pillar becomes God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead, he becomes a constituent of the New Jerusalem, and he becomes Christ in a new experiential sense—3:12.
b.　The New Jerusalem is the new Christ; as God's enlargement and expansion, we are Christ in a new sense as the New Jerusalem; the new Christ is not the same as He was in the four Gospels; the bride, who is the increase of the Bridegroom, is the New Jerusalem, including all of God's regenerated ones—John 3:29-30; Rev. 21:9-10.
c.　For us to be built into God, become a constituent of the New Jerusalem, and be-come a part of the new Christ is humanly impossible, but the law of the Spirit of life within us contains an element that deals with impossibility—Rom. 8:2; Luke 18:27; cf. Gen. 28:12-19; John 1:51.
C.　The characteristic of the overcomers in Philadelphia is their brotherly love; love prevails among them so that they shepherd people according to God (1 Pet. 5:2) by cherishing them with the cheering presence of God and nourishing them with the healthy teaching of the economy of God (Eph. 4:11; 5:29; Acts 20:28):
1.　The church life is a life of brotherly love (1 John 4:7-8; 2 John 5-6; John 15:12, 17; Rev. 3:7; Eph. 5:2; cf. Jude 12a), and the Body builds itself up in love (Eph. 4:16).
2.　The overcomers in Philadelphia stand on the genuine ground of oneness and keep themselves in the love of God to love the Lord and love all the brothers—Rev. 3:7a; cf. 2:4, 7; Jude 19-21; 2 Cor. 5:14; John 12:3; Luke 7:47; 1 John 3:14-16; Psa. 133.
3.　The overcomers in Philadelphia keep the Lord's word in His unique New Testament ministry (Rev. 3:8), which brings them into the genuine appreciation, love, and enjoyment of the precious person of the Lord Jesus Christ Himself as their life and everything (2 Cor. 11:2-3).
4.　In order to minister life to others and maintain our victory for the building up of the church, we must have a revived living and a labor in shepherding that flow out from our love for the Lord and for the brothers—Prov. 4:18; John 21:15-17.
D.　In order to continue in the way of Philadelphia, we must be saved from the way of Laodicea, which is a degraded and distorted Philadelphia—Rev. 3:14-22:
1.　Laodicea still remembers its history but has lost its former life; we must always remember that all that matters is God's present presence—Exo. 33:14; 2 Cor. 2:10.
2.　Laodicea means to know everything but in reality to be fervent about nothing; in name it has everything, but it cannot sacrifice its life for anything; it remembers its former glory but forgets its present condition before God; formerly, it was Philadelphia, but today it is Laodicea, full of lukewarmness and spiritual pride—Rev. 3:15-17.
3.　If we want to continue in the way of Philadelphia, we need to humble ourselves before God and pay the price to gain more of the Triune God as gold, white garments, and eyesalve; then we can be one with the Lord as the leading Overcomer within us in order to sit with Him on His throne in the millennial kingdom—vv. 18, 21.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第九篇　活神是爱的生活，而活在基督身体的实际里
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living a Life of God as Love
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：林前八1下，十二31下，十三1，4～8，13，十四1，3，4下，约二一15～17，启三7～22
壹　在我们的基督徒生活和召会生活中，爱必须有效能─林前十二31下，十三4～8，13：
I.　In our Christian life and church life, love must prevail—1 Cor. 12:31b; 13:4-8, 13:
一　我们必须是被基督的爱冲没并冲激的人；神圣的爱该像大水澎湃冲向我们，迫使我们情不自禁的向祂活着并爱祂到极点─林后五14。
A.　We must be persons who are flooded with and carried away by the love of Christ; the divine love should be like the rushing tide of great waters toward us, impelling us to live to Him and love Him to the uttermost beyond our own control—2 Cor. 5:14.
二　我们必须保守自己在神的爱中，并被基督的爱困迫，以至于为弟兄舍命─犹19～21，林后五14，彼前一22，约壹三14～16，四7～21。
B.　We must keep ourselves in the love of God and be constrained by the love of Christ to lay down our lives on behalf of the brothers—Jude 19-21; 2 Cor. 5:14; 1 Pet. 1:22; 1 John 3:14-16; 4:7-21.
三　我们要爱主到极点，就必须渴望并寻求一生一世住在神的殿中，瞻仰祂的荣美（可爱、可悦、可喜），在神的殿里求问神；求问神就是在我们日常生活中凡事问问神─诗二七4。
C.　In order to love the Lord to the uttermost, we need to be those who desire and seek to dwell in the house of God all the days of our life, to behold His beauty (loveliness, pleasantness, delightfulness), and to inquire of God in His temple; to inquire of God is to check with God about everything in our daily life—Psa. 27:4.
四　为着建造召会作基督生机的身体，在我们的所是和所作上，爱乃是极超越的路─林前十二31下，十三1，4～8，13：
D.　Love is the most excellent way for us to be anything or do anything for the building up of the church as the organic Body of Christ—1 Cor. 12:31b; 13:1, 4-8, 13:
1　保罗在林前十三章所描述的爱，乃是神圣生命的彰显（4～8上）；不仅如此，爱乃是那灵的果子，这指明爱的本质必须是那灵（加五22）；我们若没有爱，我们的说话就如同鸣的锣、响的钹，发出声音却没有生命（林前十三1，十四1，3，4下，12，31，林后三6）。─引用经文
1.　The love described by Paul in 1 Corinthians 13 is the expression of the divine life (vv. 4-8a); furthermore, the fact that love is the fruit of the Spirit indicates that the substance of love must be the Spirit (Gal. 5:22); if we do not have love, our speaking is like that of sounding brass and a clanging cymbal, which give sounds without life (1 Cor. 13:1; 14:1, 3, 4b, 12, 31; 2 Cor. 3:6).
2　我们在爱别人的事上，应当像神一样，一无分别的爱人（太五43～48）；基督借着钉十字架而拯救的第一个人，不是一个绅士，而是一个罪犯，一个判处死刑的强盗；这是非常有意义的（二七38，路二三42～43）。─引用经文
2.　We should be like God in our love for others, loving people without any discrimination (Matt. 5:43-48); the first one saved by Christ through His crucifixion was not a gentleman but a criminal, a robber, sentenced to death; this is very meaningful (27:38; Luke 23:42-43).
3　当生命之灵的律作为爱的律在我们里面得以发动，我们就自动并自然的成为牧人，有我们父神爱和赦免的心，并我们救主基督牧养和寻找的灵─罗八2，加六2～3，约二一15～17，路十五3～7。
3.　When the law of the Spirit of life as the law of love is activated within us, we automatically and spontaneously will be shepherds who have the loving and forgiving heart of our Father God and the shepherding and seeking spirit of our Savior Christ— Rom. 8:2; Gal. 6:2-3; John 21:15-17; Luke 15:3-7.
4　我们在主里的劳苦乃是爱心的劳苦（林前十五58，帖前一3）；在其中我们“扶助软弱的人”（徒二十35）并“扶持软弱的人”（帖前五14）；“软弱的人”指那些在灵、魂、体方面软弱，或是在信心上软弱的人（罗十四1，十五1）。─引用经文
4.　Our labor in the Lord is a labor of love (1 Cor. 15:58; 1 Thes. 1:3) in which we "support the weak" (Acts 20:35) and "sustain the weak" (1 Thes. 5:14); the weak refers to those who are weak either in their spirit, soul, or body, or are weak in faith (Rom. 14:1; 15:1).
五　“知识是叫人自高自大，惟有爱建造人”；我们可能听了职事的信息，只得了一些知识，就自高自大─林前八1下，参林后三6。
E.　"Knowledge puffs up, but love builds up"; we may listen to the messages of the ministry and become puffed up with mere knowledge—1 Cor. 8:1b; cf. 2 Cor. 3:6.
贰　主现今并终极恢复之现有的真理，乃是借着我们拣选走非拉铁非的路，将我们带进新的复兴，以转移时代；惟有恢复的召会，就是在非拉铁非的召会所表征之弟兄相爱的召会，才能成就神永远的定旨，并满足祂心头的愿望─启一1～3，三7～13，诗歌六四〇首：
II.　The present truth of the Lord's up-to-date and ultimate recovery is to bring us into a new revival to turn the age by our choosing to take the way of Philadelphia; only the recovered church, the church of brotherly love, signified by the church in Philadelphia, can fulfill God's eternal purpose and satisfy His heart's desire— Rev. 1:1-3; 3:7-13; Hymns, #880:
一　在非拉铁非的得胜者（7～13），其特征是他们渴望达到神经纶之神圣启示的最高峰─这最高峰就是神成为人，为要使人在生命和性情上，但不在神格上，成为神，使基督的身体得以产生，基督的新妇得以预备好，新耶路撒冷得以终极完成：
A.　The characteristic of the overcomers in Philadelphia (vv. 7-13) is their aspiration to arrive at the highest peak of the divine revelation of God's economy—this highest peak is God becoming man to make man God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead so that the Body of Christ can be produced, the bride can be prepared, and the New Jerusalem can be consummated:
1　虽然普遍说来，在亚西亚的众召会离弃了使徒保罗的职事（提后一15），但有一个召会是独特的，非常受主称赞─在非拉铁非的召会；主非常称赞他们，甚至珍赏他们，因为他们遵守主的话，那就是说，他们没有离弃使徒保罗关于神经纶之健康教训的话语，就是神圣启示的最高峰（启三8，提前一3～4，六3）。─引用经文
1.　Even though the churches in Asia, in a general sense, had turned away from the apostle Paul's ministry (2 Tim. 1:15), one church was unique and was highly appraised by the Lord—the church in Philadelphia; the Lord highly appraised them and even appreciated them because they kept His word, which means that they did not turn away from the word of the apostle Paul's healthy teaching of God's economy, the highest peak of the divine revelation (Rev. 3:8; 1 Tim. 1:3-4; 6:3).
2　那些在非拉铁非的人，借着祷读并默想神的话，将祂的话珍藏在心里（弗六17～18，诗一一九11，15），“对神〔是〕富足的”（路十二21）；他们向神的话举手，指明他们热诚欢乐的接受它，并对它说，阿们（诗一一九48，尼八5～6）。─引用经文
2.　Those in Philadelphia are "rich toward God" (Luke 12:21) by pray-reading and musing upon His word to treasure up His word in their heart (Eph. 6:17-18; Psa. 119:11, 15); they lift up their hands unto the word of God, indicating that they receive it warmly and gladly and that they say Amen to it (v. 48; Neh. 8:5-6).
3　得胜者在殿中作柱子，意思就是他们要在三一神里作柱子，因为殿就是“主神全能者和羔羊”；神建造到他们里面，使他们成为宝贵的石头，他们也建造到神里面，使他们成为在神里面的石柱，他们就与神合并，作神与人相互的住处─启三12上，二一22，3，诗九十1，约十四23，参王上七17。
3.　For the overcomers to be pillars in the temple means that they will be pillars in the Triune God, for the temple is "the Lord God the Almighty and the Lamb"; God is built into them to make them precious stones, and they are built into God to make them pillars of stone in God for their incorporation with God as the mutual abode of God and man—Rev. 3:12a; 21:22, 3; Psa. 90:1; John 14:23; cf. 1 Kings 7:17.
4　将神的名，新耶路撒冷的名，并主的新名，写在得胜者上面，指明神的所是、新耶路撒冷的性质并主的人位，全都作到他们里面，使他们有三一神为标示，作他们的“名牌”，并使他们在生命和性情上成为神，但无分于神格─启三12下，二4下。
4.　That the name of God, the name of the New Jerusalem, and the Lord's new name are written upon the overcomers indicates that what God is, the nature of the New Jerusalem, and the person of the Lord have all been wrought into them, labeling them with the Triune God as their "name badge" and making them God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead—Rev. 3:12b; 22:4b.
二　在非拉铁非的得胜者，其特征是他们借着享受基督的丰富作他们内住的宝贝，而竭力进入神人的生活─三7，赛二二15，20～24：
B.　The characteristic of the overcomers in Philadelphia is their endeavoring to enter into the God-man living by enjoying the riches of Christ as their indwelling treasure—Eph. 3:8; 2 Cor. 4:7:
1　在以赛亚二十二章，神解雇舍伯那，就是王家里的家宰（15～19），而用预表包罗万有之基督的以利亚敬顶替；基督是神家的管家，乃是肩头上放着神家之钥匙的一位（20～25，启三7～8）；基督有支配神宝库之门的钥匙，在这宝库中，有神在基督里的丰富作我们的享受（帖前五16～19，参结一22，26）：─引用经文
1.　In Isaiah 22 God fired Shebna, a steward in the house of the king (vv. 15-19), and replaced him with Eliakim, a type of the all-inclusive Christ as the Steward in God's house, the One upon whose shoulder the key of the house of God is set (vv. 20-25; Rev. 3:7-8); Christ has the key to control the door of God's treasury, in which are the riches of God in Christ for our enjoyment (1 Thes. 5:16-19; cf. Ezek. 1:22, 26):
a　真正的召会生活，乃是众圣徒都被解雇，而被基督顶替，使基督在召会中成为一切的生活；我们众人都是“舍伯那”，该被基督这真以利亚敬除去并顶替，使我们成为祂这位神奥秘与神诸般恩典之管家的复制─西三10～11，林前四1，彼前四10。
a.　The real church life is a life in which all the saints are fired and replaced with Christ, making Christ everything in the church; all of us are Shebnas, who should be removed and replaced by Christ as the real Eliakim to make us His duplication as stewards of the mysteries of God and the varied grace of God— Col. 3:10-11; 1 Cor. 4:1; 1 Pet. 4:10.
b　因着我们已经与基督联合，基督也使祂自己与我们联合，与我们联结，所以当祂死在十字架上时，我们就与祂同死，且被了结；如今在我们与基督生机的联结中，祂活在我们里面，与我们同活，借着我们并经过我们而活，因而顶替了我们─罗六6，加二20，罗八16，林前六17。
b.　Because we have been joined to Christ, and Christ joined Himself to us, uniting Himself with us, when He died on the cross, we died with Him and were terminated; now in our organic union with Christ, He replaces us by living in us, with us, by us, and through us—Rom. 6:6; Gal. 2:20; Rom. 8:16; 1 Cor. 6:17.
2　主用大卫的钥匙开启扩展祂恢复的门，对我们是客观的，但基督也用大卫的钥匙主观的开启我们里面之人的门，使我们变化并建造成为神的殿，作柱子，有神的名，新耶路撒冷的名，并主的新名─启二17，三12，参二一22：
2.　The Lord's using the key of David to open the door for the spread of His recovery is objective to us, but Christ is also using the key of David to subjectively open the door in our inner being for us to be transformed and built into the house of God as a pillar with the name of God, the name of the New Jerusalem, and the new name of the Lord—Rev. 2:17; 3:12; cf. 21:22:
a　“我神的名”指明柱子是神；“我神城的名”指明柱子是新耶路撒冷；“我的新名”指明柱子是具有新意义的基督；得胜者作为柱子，成为神（在生命和性情上，但无分于神格）、成为新耶路撒冷的构成分子、并成为在新的经历意义上的基督─三12。
a.　The name of My God indicates that the pillar is God; the name of the city of My God indicates that the pillar is the New Jerusalem; and My new name indicates that the pillar is Christ in a new significance; the overcomer as a pillar becomes God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead, he becomes a constituent of the New Jerusalem, and he becomes Christ in a new experiential sense—3:12.
b　新耶路撒冷乃是新的基督；我们作为神的扩大和扩展，乃是具有新意义的基督，就是新耶路撒冷；新的基督与祂在四福音书里不一样；新妇作为新郎的扩增，乃是新耶路撒冷，包括所有由神重生的人─约三29～30，启二一9～10。
b.　The New Jerusalem is the new Christ; as God's enlargement and expansion, we are Christ in a new sense as the New Jerusalem; the new Christ is not the same as He was in the four Gospels; the bride, who is the increase of the Bridegroom, is the New Jerusalem, including all of God's regenerated ones—John 3:29-30; Rev. 21:9-10.
c　我们要被建造到神里面，成为新耶路撒冷的构成成分，并成为新的基督的一部分，就人说是不可能的，但我们里面生命之灵的律包含一个元素，能对付不可能─罗八2，路十八27，参创二八12～19，约一51。
c.　For us to be built into God, become a constituent of the New Jerusalem, and be-come a part of the new Christ is humanly impossible, but the law of the Spirit of life within us contains an element that deals with impossibility—Rom. 8:2; Luke 18:27; cf. Gen. 28:12-19; John 1:51.
三　在非拉铁非的得胜者，其特征是弟兄相爱；在他们中间，爱是有效能的，以致他们按着神牧养人（彼前五2），以令人愉快之神的同在顾惜人，并以神经纶健康的教训喂养人（弗四11，五29，徒二十28）：─引用经文
C.　The characteristic of the overcomers in Philadelphia is their brotherly love; love prevails among them so that they shepherd people according to God (1 Pet. 5:2) by cherishing them with the cheering presence of God and nourishing them with the healthy teaching of the economy of God (Eph. 4:11; 5:29; Acts 20:28):
1　召会生活乃是弟兄相爱的生活（约壹四7～8，约贰5～6，约十五12，17，启三7，弗五2，参犹12上），并且身体在爱里把自己建造起来（弗四16）。─引用经文
1.　The church life is a life of brotherly love (1 John 4:7-8; 2 John 5-6; John 15:12, 17; Rev. 3:7; Eph. 5:2; cf. Jude 12a), and the Body builds itself up in love (Eph. 4:16).
2　在非拉铁非的得胜者站在一的真正立场上，并保守自己在神的爱里，爱主并爱所有的弟兄们─启三7上，参二4，7，犹19～21，林后五14，约十二3，路七47，约壹三14～16，诗一三三。
2.　The overcomers in Philadelphia stand on the genuine ground of oneness and keep themselves in the love of God to love the Lord and love all the brothers—Rev. 3:7a; cf. 2:4, 7; Jude 19-21; 2 Cor. 5:14; John 12:3; Luke 7:47; 1 John 3:14-16; Psa. 133.
3　在非拉铁非的得胜者持守主在祂独一新约职事里的话（启三8），这话将他们带进对作他们的生命和一切之主耶稣基督自己这宝贵人位的真实珍赏、爱和享受里（林后十一2～3）。─引用经文
3.　The overcomers in Philadelphia keep the Lord's word in His unique New Testament ministry (Rev. 3:8), which brings them into the genuine appreciation, love, and enjoyment of the precious person of the Lord Jesus Christ Himself as their life and everything (2 Cor. 11:2-3).
4　我们要将生命供应给人，并维持我们的得胜，以建造召会，就必须从我们对主的爱和对弟兄们的爱，涌流出复兴的生活并在牧养上的劳苦─箴四18，约二一15～17。
4.　In order to minister life to others and maintain our victory for the building up of the church, we must have a revived living and a labor in shepherding that flow out from our love for the Lord and for the brothers—Prov. 4:18; John 21:15-17.
四　我们若要持续走非拉铁非的路，就必须蒙拯救脱离老底嘉的路，也就是堕落并走了样的非拉铁非─启三14～22：
D.　In order to continue in the way of Philadelphia, we must be saved from the way of Laodicea, which is a degraded and distorted Philadelphia—Rev. 3:14-22:
1　老底嘉记得自己已往的故事，但是已往的生命没有了；我们必须一直记住，重要的乃是神现今的同在─出三三14，林后二10。
1.　Laodicea still remembers its history but has lost its former life; we must always remember that all that matters is God's present presence—Exo. 33:14; 2 Cor. 2:10.
2　老底嘉，就是说起来样样都知道，事实上没有一样是热切的；说起来样样都有，但是没有一样是能够把命拚上的；记得已往时候的光荣，却忘记了今天在神面前的光景；已往是非拉铁非，今天是老底嘉，满了不冷不热和属灵的骄傲─启三15～17。
2.　Laodicea means to know everything but in reality to be fervent about nothing; in name it has everything, but it cannot sacrifice its life for anything; it remembers its former glory but forgets its present condition before God; formerly, it was Philadelphia, but today it is Laodicea, full of lukewarmness and spiritual pride—Rev. 3:15-17.
3　我们如果要继续在非拉铁非的道路上，就得在神面前谦卑自己，并付代价得着更多三一神作金子、白衣和眼药；这样，我们就能与主这位在我们里面领头的得胜者是一，好在千年国里与祂一同坐在祂的宝座上─18，21节。
3.　If we want to continue in the way of Philadelphia, we need to humble ourselves before God and pay the price to gain more of the Triune God as gold, white garments, and eyesalve; then we can be one with the Lord as the leading Overcomer within us in order to sit with Him on His throne in the millennial kingdom—vv. 18, 21.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十篇　经历基督是祭物的实际，而活在基督身体的实际里
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：林后五21，彼前二24，约六57，林前十17，林后一9，弗一21，二14～17，腓二17，来二17～18，四14～16，十5～10，启一18，二8
壹　基督是一切祭物的应验、顶替和实际─来十5～10。
贰　基督是赎罪祭的实际，替我们成为罪，死在十字架上，对付我们堕落之人的罪性─林后五21，罗八3，约三14：
一　基督为我们成为罪，好在十字架上借着死定罪了罪─利四1～3，13～14，22～23，27～28。
二　借着基督在蛇的形状里受死，那在人的肉体里之撒但的邪恶性情就在十字架上受了审判，使信徒可以得着永远的生命─约三14～16，一14，罗八3。
三　基督是那不知罪的，替我们成为罪，好叫我们在祂里面成为神的义─林后五21。
叁　基督是赎愆祭的实际，在自己的身体里担当了我们的诸罪，在十字架上受神审判，对付我们的罪行，使我们罪的行为得着赦免─彼前二24，三18：
一　取用基督作我们的赎愆祭，承认我们的罪，乃是维持我们在生命的交通中，使我们在生命里长大，达到生命成熟的路─约壹一2～3，5～9，徒二四16。
二　取用基督作我们的赎愆祭，使我们的罪得着赦免，结果使我们敬畏神并爱神─诗一三○4，路七47～50。
肆　那作为神的食物完全为着神满足的燔祭，表征基督是神的喜悦和满足，祂在地上的生活绝对为着神─利一3，民二八2～3，约五30，六38，八29：
一　借着按手在作燔祭的基督身上，我们就与祂联结，祂与我们就成为一；在这样的联合里，我们一切的软弱、缺陷和过失，都由祂担负，祂一切的美德都成为我们的─加二20上。
二　我们需要天天取用基督作我们的燔祭，使我们可以在基督作燔祭的经历上经历祂，并不是在外面模仿祂，乃是在日常生活中活祂─利一2～4，六12～13，参提后二6，林后五14～15，腓一19～21，徒二七22～25。
伍　基督是素祭的实际，在祂完美的人性里是神的食物，也是那些与神交通并事奉神之人的食物─约七46，十八38，十九4，6：
一　素祭预表基督在祂的人性里是神的食物，特别是那些与神交通并事奉神之人的食物─利二2～4。
二　我们若吃基督作素祭，就会成为我们所吃的，并且凭我们所吃的而活─约六57，林前十17。
三　我们是在基督里的信徒和基督的肢体，该是基督作素祭的复制─林后四10～11，林前十17。
陆　基督是平安祭的实际，是成就和平者，为我们受死，作了我们与神之间的和平─弗二14～15：
一　享受基督作我们的赎罪祭、赎愆祭、燔祭和素祭的结果，乃是享受基督作平安祭─利三1～2，六12，七37。
二　基督是神与祂子民之间的平安，作他们的共同享受─参林前一9。
三　为着基督的身体，我们需要经历基督作平安祭─弗二14～17，四3，六15，西一20～22，三15。
四　我们在召会生活里需要在每一件事上，在每一方面，与每一个人都有平安；为此，我们需要平安的主随时多方赐我们平安─来十二14，帖前五13下，帖后三16。
柒　基督是摇祭的实际，是复活、活的一位─启一18，徒二24：
一　摇祭预表基督是复活、活的一位─利七30，二三10～11，启一18，二8。
二　我们是基督身体的肢体，需要经历在复活里的基督并被带到复活里─弗二5～6，腓三10～11。
三　神一直借着十字架作工，了结我们，领我们到尽头，使我们不再信靠自己，只信靠复活的神─林后一9。
捌　基督是举祭的实际，是在升天和高举里有能力的一位─弗一21：
一　举祭是在主面前举起来的祭，预表在升天和高举里的基督，就是“远超过一切”的那一位─利七14，32，弗一21。
二　在基督的高举里，神已使基督向着召会作万有的头─22～23节。
三　基督在祂升天的天上职事里，在神面前担负我们，并照着神所要的照顾我们一切的需要─来二17～18，四14～16。
玖　基督是奠祭的实际，是在神前，像酒一样倾倒出来，使神得着满足的那一位─腓二17：
一　奠祭预表基督是真正的酒在神前倾倒出来，使神满足的那一位─出二九40～41。
二　葡萄树描述献祭的基督，就是将祂自己的一切全献上的基督；本于祂的献祭，祂产生了新酒，使神和人喜乐─士九13。
三　奠祭不仅预表基督自己，也预表这位基督以祂自己作属天的酒浸透我们，直到祂与我们成为一而被浇奠给神，为着神的享受和满足，并为着神的建造─太九17，腓二17，提后四6。

页首-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
LIVING IN THE REALITY OF THE BODY OF CHRIST BY LEARNING CHRIST AS THE REALITY IS IN JESUS
Message Ten
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Experiencing Christ as the Reality of the Offerings
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: 2 Cor. 5:21; 1 Pet. 2:24; John 6:57; 1 Cor. 10:17; 2 Cor. 1:9; Eph. 1:21; 2:14-17; Phil. 2:17; Heb. 2:17-18; 4:14-16; 10:5-10; Rev. 1:18; 2:8
I.　Christ is the fulfillment, the replacement, and the reality of all the offerings— Heb. 10:5-10.
II.　As the reality of the sin offering, Christ was made sin on our behalf and died on the cross to deal with the sinful nature of our fallen being—2 Cor. 5:21; Rom. 8:3; John 3:14:
A.　Christ was made sin for us so that through His death on the cross sin might be condemned—Lev. 4:1-3, 13-14, 22-23, 27-28.
B.　Satan's evil nature in man's flesh was judged on the cross through the death of Christ in the form of a serpent so that the believers may have eternal life—John 3:14-16; 1:14; Rom. 8:3.
C.　As the One who did not know sin, Christ was made sin on our behalf for us to become the righteousness of God in Him—2 Cor. 5:21.
III.　As the reality of the trespass offering, Christ bore up our sins in His own body and was judged by God on the cross to deal with our sinful deeds that we might be forgiven in our sinful conduct—1 Pet. 2:24; 3:18:
A.　Taking Christ as our trespass offering with the confession of our sins is the way to keep ourselves in the fellowship of life for our growth in life unto the maturity in life—1 John 1:2-3, 5-9; Acts 24:16.
B.　Taking Christ as our trespass offering to receive forgiveness of sins issues in our fearing God and loving God—Psa. 130:4; Luke 7:47-50.
IV.　The burnt offering, which was wholly for God's satisfaction, as food for God, signifies Christ as God's pleasure and satisfaction, as the One whose living on earth was absolutely for God—Lev. 1:3; Num. 28:2-3; John 5:30; 6:38; 8:29:
A.　By laying our hands on Christ as the burnt offering, we are joined to Him, and He and we become one; in such a union, all our weaknesses, defects, and faults are taken on by Him, and all His virtues become ours—Gal. 2:20a.
B.　We need to take Christ as our burnt offering daily so that we may experience Christ in His experience as a burnt offering, not imitating Christ outwardly but living Him in our daily life—Lev. 1:2-4; 6:12-13; cf. 2 Tim. 2:6; 2 Cor. 5:14-15; Phil. 1:19-21; Acts 27:22-25.
V.　As the reality of the meal offering, Christ in His perfect humanity is food for God and for those who have fellowship with God and serve Him—John 7:46; 18:38; 19:4, 6:
A.　The meal offering typifies Christ in His humanity as food for God and especially for those who have fellowship with Him and serve Him—Lev. 2:2-4.
B.　If we eat Christ as the meal offering, we will become what we eat and live by what we eat—John 6:57; 1 Cor. 10:17.
C.　As believers in Christ and members of Christ, we should be the reproduction of Christ as the meal offering—2 Cor. 4:10-11; 1 Cor. 10:17.
VI.　As the reality of the peace offering, Christ is the Peacemaker, the One who became the peace between us and God by dying for us—Eph. 2:14-15:
A.　The issue of enjoying Christ as our sin offering, our trespass offering, our burnt offering, and our meal offering is the enjoyment of Christ as the peace offering—Lev. 3:1-2; 6:12; 7:37.
B.　Christ is the peace between God and God's people for their co-enjoyment—cf. 1 Cor. 1:9.
C.　We need to experience Christ as the peace offering for the Body of Christ—Eph. 2:14-17; 4:3; 6:15; Col. 1:20-22; 3:15.
D.　In the church life, we need to be at peace in everything, in every way, and with everyone; for this we need the Lord of peace to give us peace continually in every way— Heb. 12:14; 1 Thes. 5:13b; 2 Thes. 3:16.
VII.　As the reality of the wave offering, Christ is the resurrected, living One—Rev. 1:18; Acts 2:24:
A.　The wave offering typifies Christ as the resurrected, living One—Lev. 7:30; 23:10-11; Rev. 1:18; 2:8.
B.　As members of the Body, we need to experience Christ in His resurrection and be brought into resurrection—Eph. 2:5-6; Phil. 3:10-11.
C.　God is working through the cross to terminate us, to bring us to an end, so that we will no longer trust in ourselves but in the God of resurrection—2 Cor. 1:9.
VIII.　As the reality of the heave offering, Christ is the powerful One in ascension and exaltation—Eph. 1:21:
A.　The heave offering, an offering heaved up before the Lord, typifies Christ in ascension and exaltation, the One who is "far above all"—Lev. 7:14, 32; Eph. 1:21.
B.　In His ascension Christ was given to be the Head over all things to the church—vv. 22-23.
C.　In His heavenly ministry in ascension, Christ is bearing us in the presence of God and caring for all our needs according to God's desire—Heb. 2:17-18; 4:14-16.
IX.　As the reality of the drink offering, Christ is the One who was poured out as wine before God for His satisfaction—Phil. 2:17:
A.　The drink offering typifies Christ as the One poured out as the real wine before God for His satisfaction—Exo. 29:40-41.
B.　The vine depicts the sacrificing Christ, the Christ who sacrificed everything of Himself, and out of His sacrifice He produced new wine to cheer God and man—Judg. 9:13.
C.　The drink offering typifies not only Christ Himself but also the Christ who saturates us with Himself as heavenly wine until He and we become one to be poured out for God's enjoyment and satisfaction and for God's building—Matt. 9:17; Phil. 2:17; 2 Tim. 4:6.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十篇　经历基督是祭物的实际，而活在基督身体的实际里
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Experiencing Christ as the Reality of the Offerings
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：林后五21，彼前二24，约六57，林前十17，林后一9，弗一21，二14～17，腓二17，来二17～18，四14～16，十5～10，启一18，二8
壹　基督是一切祭物的应验、顶替和实际─来十5～10。
I.　Christ is the fulfillment, the replacement, and the reality of all the offerings— Heb. 10:5-10.
贰　基督是赎罪祭的实际，替我们成为罪，死在十字架上，对付我们堕落之人的罪性─林后五21，罗八3，约三14：
II.　As the reality of the sin offering, Christ was made sin on our behalf and died on the cross to deal with the sinful nature of our fallen being—2 Cor. 5:21; Rom. 8:3; John 3:14:
一　基督为我们成为罪，好在十字架上借着死定罪了罪─利四1～3，13～14，22～23，27～28。
A.　Christ was made sin for us so that through His death on the cross sin might be condemned—Lev. 4:1-3, 13-14, 22-23, 27-28.
二　借着基督在蛇的形状里受死，那在人的肉体里之撒但的邪恶性情就在十字架上受了审判，使信徒可以得着永远的生命─约三14～16，一14，罗八3。
B.　Satan's evil nature in man's flesh was judged on the cross through the death of Christ in the form of a serpent so that the believers may have eternal life—John 3:14-16; 1:14; Rom. 8:3.
三　基督是那不知罪的，替我们成为罪，好叫我们在祂里面成为神的义─林后五21。
C.　As the One who did not know sin, Christ was made sin on our behalf for us to become the righteousness of God in Him—2 Cor. 5:21.
叁　基督是赎愆祭的实际，在自己的身体里担当了我们的诸罪，在十字架上受神审判，对付我们的罪行，使我们罪的行为得着赦免─彼前二24，三18：
III.　As the reality of the trespass offering, Christ bore up our sins in His own body and was judged by God on the cross to deal with our sinful deeds that we might be forgiven in our sinful conduct—1 Pet. 2:24; 3:18:
一　取用基督作我们的赎愆祭，承认我们的罪，乃是维持我们在生命的交通中，使我们在生命里长大，达到生命成熟的路─约壹一2～3，5～9，徒二四16。
A.　Taking Christ as our trespass offering with the confession of our sins is the way to keep ourselves in the fellowship of life for our growth in life unto the maturity in life—1 John 1:2-3, 5-9; Acts 24:16.
二　取用基督作我们的赎愆祭，使我们的罪得着赦免，结果使我们敬畏神并爱神─诗一三○4，路七47～50。
B.　Taking Christ as our trespass offering to receive forgiveness of sins issues in our fearing God and loving God—Psa. 130:4; Luke 7:47-50.
肆　那作为神的食物完全为着神满足的燔祭，表征基督是神的喜悦和满足，祂在地上的生活绝对为着神─利一3，民二八2～3，约五30，六38，八29：
IV.　The burnt offering, which was wholly for God's satisfaction, as food for God, signifies Christ as God's pleasure and satisfaction, as the One whose living on earth was absolutely for God—Lev. 1:3; Num. 28:2-3; John 5:30; 6:38; 8:29:
一　借着按手在作燔祭的基督身上，我们就与祂联结，祂与我们就成为一；在这样的联合里，我们一切的软弱、缺陷和过失，都由祂担负，祂一切的美德都成为我们的─加二20上。
A.　By laying our hands on Christ as the burnt offering, we are joined to Him, and He and we become one; in such a union, all our weaknesses, defects, and faults are taken on by Him, and all His virtues become ours—Gal. 2:20a.
二　我们需要天天取用基督作我们的燔祭，使我们可以在基督作燔祭的经历上经历祂，并不是在外面模仿祂，乃是在日常生活中活祂─利一2～4，六12～13，参提后二6，林后五14～15，腓一19～21，徒二七22～25。
B.　We need to take Christ as our burnt offering daily so that we may experience Christ in His experience as a burnt offering, not imitating Christ outwardly but living Him in our daily life—Lev. 1:2-4; 6:12-13; cf. 2 Tim. 2:6; 2 Cor. 5:14-15; Phil. 1:19-21; Acts 27:22-25.
伍　基督是素祭的实际，在祂完美的人性里是神的食物，也是那些与神交通并事奉神之人的食物─约七46，十八38，十九4，6：
V.　As the reality of the meal offering, Christ in His perfect humanity is food for God and for those who have fellowship with God and serve Him—John 7:46; 18:38; 19:4, 6:
一　素祭预表基督在祂的人性里是神的食物，特别是那些与神交通并事奉神之人的食物─利二2～4。
A.　The meal offering typifies Christ in His humanity as food for God and especially for those who have fellowship with Him and serve Him—Lev. 2:2-4.
二　我们若吃基督作素祭，就会成为我们所吃的，并且凭我们所吃的而活─约六57，林前十17。
B.　If we eat Christ as the meal offering, we will become what we eat and live by what we eat—John 6:57; 1 Cor. 10:17.
三　我们是在基督里的信徒和基督的肢体，该是基督作素祭的复制─林后四10～11，林前十17。
C.　As believers in Christ and members of Christ, we should be the reproduction of Christ as the meal offering—2 Cor. 4:10-11; 1 Cor. 10:17.
陆　基督是平安祭的实际，是成就和平者，为我们受死，作了我们与神之间的和平─弗二14～15：
VI.　As the reality of the peace offering, Christ is the Peacemaker, the One who became the peace between us and God by dying for us—Eph. 2:14-15:
一　享受基督作我们的赎罪祭、赎愆祭、燔祭和素祭的结果，乃是享受基督作平安祭─利三1～2，六12，七37。
A.　The issue of enjoying Christ as our sin offering, our trespass offering, our burnt offering, and our meal offering is the enjoyment of Christ as the peace offering—Lev. 3:1-2; 6:12; 7:37.
二　基督是神与祂子民之间的平安，作他们的共同享受─参林前一9。
B.　Christ is the peace between God and God's people for their co-enjoyment—cf. 1 Cor. 1:9.
三　为着基督的身体，我们需要经历基督作平安祭─弗二14～17，四3，六15，西一20～22，三15。
C.　We need to experience Christ as the peace offering for the Body of Christ—Eph. 2:14-17; 4:3; 6:15; Col. 1:20-22; 3:15.
四　我们在召会生活里需要在每一件事上，在每一方面，与每一个人都有平安；为此，我们需要平安的主随时多方赐我们平安─来十二14，帖前五13下，帖后三16。
D.　In the church life, we need to be at peace in everything, in every way, and with everyone; for this we need the Lord of peace to give us peace continually in every way— Heb. 12:14; 1 Thes. 5:13b; 2 Thes. 3:16.
柒　基督是摇祭的实际，是复活、活的一位─启一18，徒二24：
VII.　As the reality of the wave offering, Christ is the resurrected, living One—Rev. 1:18; Acts 2:24:
一　摇祭预表基督是复活、活的一位─利七30，二三10～11，启一18，二8。
A.　The wave offering typifies Christ as the resurrected, living One—Lev. 7:30; 23:10-11; Rev. 1:18; 2:8.
二　我们是基督身体的肢体，需要经历在复活里的基督并被带到复活里─弗二5～6，腓三10～11。
B.　As members of the Body, we need to experience Christ in His resurrection and be brought into resurrection—Eph. 2:5-6; Phil. 3:10-11.
三　神一直借着十字架作工，了结我们，领我们到尽头，使我们不再信靠自己，只信靠复活的神─林后一9。
C.　God is working through the cross to terminate us, to bring us to an end, so that we will no longer trust in ourselves but in the God of resurrection—2 Cor. 1:9.
捌　基督是举祭的实际，是在升天和高举里有能力的一位─弗一21：
VIII.　As the reality of the heave offering, Christ is the powerful One in ascension and exaltation—Eph. 1:21:
一　举祭是在主面前举起来的祭，预表在升天和高举里的基督，就是“远超过一切”的那一位─利七14，32，弗一21。
A.　The heave offering, an offering heaved up before the Lord, typifies Christ in ascension and exaltation, the One who is "far above all"—Lev. 7:14, 32; Eph. 1:21.
二　在基督的高举里，神已使基督向着召会作万有的头─22～23节。
B.　In His ascension Christ was given to be the Head over all things to the church—vv. 22-23.
三　基督在祂升天的天上职事里，在神面前担负我们，并照着神所要的照顾我们一切的需要─来二17～18，四14～16。
C.　In His heavenly ministry in ascension, Christ is bearing us in the presence of God and caring for all our needs according to God's desire—Heb. 2:17-18; 4:14-16.
玖　基督是奠祭的实际，是在神前，像酒一样倾倒出来，使神得着满足的那一位─腓二17：
IX.　As the reality of the drink offering, Christ is the One who was poured out as wine before God for His satisfaction—Phil. 2:17:
一　奠祭预表基督是真正的酒在神前倾倒出来，使神满足的那一位─出二九40～41。
A.　The drink offering typifies Christ as the One poured out as the real wine before God for His satisfaction—Exo. 29:40-41.
二　葡萄树描述献祭的基督，就是将祂自己的一切全献上的基督；本于祂的献祭，祂产生了新酒，使神和人喜乐─士九13。
B.　The vine depicts the sacrificing Christ, the Christ who sacrificed everything of Himself, and out of His sacrifice He produced new wine to cheer God and man—Judg. 9:13.
三　奠祭不仅预表基督自己，也预表这位基督以祂自己作属天的酒浸透我们，直到祂与我们成为一而被浇奠给神，为着神的享受和满足，并为着神的建造─太九17，腓二17，提后四6。
C.　The drink offering typifies not only Christ Himself but also the Christ who saturates us with Himself as heavenly wine until He and we become one to be poured out for God's enjoyment and satisfaction and for God's building—Matt. 9:17; Phil. 2:17; 2 Tim. 4:6.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十一篇　活在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，而活在基督身体的实际里
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：约一14，三3，5，13，七39，十四1，10～11，十六33，来四12，太二四40～41
壹　约翰福音是一卷奥秘的书，约翰福音的全部记载也是神圣奥秘生命之奥秘的记载，启示神圣奥秘的范围─一1，14，三3，5，13，十四1，十六33：
一　约翰福音是由一位神圣奥秘的人所写神圣奥秘的书，陈明三一神与终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘范围的异象。
二　主恢复里所有的圣徒，都需要对于物质的范围和神圣奥秘的范围有清楚的看见─弗一17～23。
三　我们需要进入一个范围，是远高于物质的范围；这高得多的范围，就是神圣奥秘的范围。
贰　三一神自己就是神圣奥秘的范围；神圣三一的三者乃是自有永有的，同时并存，且互相内在；因此，父、子、灵就是一个神圣奥秘的范围─约十四10～11，太二八19，林后十三14。
叁　我们需要活在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里─约七39，加三14，罗八9，林后三17～18：
一　复合的膏油所预表终极完成的灵，乃是神圣奥秘的范围；我们应当学习活在这范围里─出三十22～33，约壹二20，27。
二　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们接受那灵作独一、包罗万有的福─加三14，2，5。
三　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们接受升天基督的输供和祂天上职事的供应─弗一22，来八1~2。
四　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们经历神生机的拯救─罗五10。
五　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们照着生命之律的自动功用，过着自然而毫不费力的基督徒生活─八2。
六　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们成为神圣奥秘的人，同时活在物质的范围和神圣奥秘的范围里─约三13，来四16，十三13。
七　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们过真实的生活，彰显那启示出来的神圣实际─约贰1，约参3，约四23～24。
八　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们活在神的国这神圣种类的范围里─三3，5。
九　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们活在神圣的交通里；这是活在基督身体里的实际─约壹一3，7，徒二42，罗十二5。
十　在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，我们与三一神调和，为着保守一─约十七21，弗四3～6：
1　真正的一乃是在三一神里─约十七21：
a　信徒的一，实际上乃是三一神的一。
b　惟有在三一神里，我们才能被成全成为一─23节。
2　真正的一乃是信徒与三一神的调和─弗三14～四6：
a　我们要有这一，就必须在三一神这神圣奥秘的范围里。
b　信徒乃是在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，与三一神是一─加三14，罗八9，林后三17～18。
肆　在我们的经历里，我们实际上成为神圣奥秘范围的一部分─约十四2～3，十五1，4，弗四4～6：
一　我们借着重生而成为神圣奥秘范围的一部分，借此我们生入神圣奥秘的范围里─约三5～6。
二　我们借着有分于神的生命（15，西三4）、性情（弗一4，彼后一4）、心思（弗四23，腓二5）、所是（林后三18下，弗三8）、形像（林后三18上，罗八29）、荣耀（30，来二10）、儿子名分（弗一5，罗八23）、显明（19）、和样式（约壹三2），而成为神圣奥秘范围的一部分。─引用经文
三　我们借着建造到基督的身体里而成为神圣奥秘范围的一部分；这身体要完成新耶路撒冷─弗四16，启二一2，10～11：
1　基督的身体乃是神圣奥秘的范围；我们越在基督身体的实际里，就越在神圣奥秘的范围里─罗十二4～5，林前十二12～13，27，弗一22～23，四16。
2　基督的身体要完成新耶路撒冷，作新天新地里神圣奥秘的范围，直到永远─启二一1～2，10～11。
伍　我们若要活在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，并成为终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘范围的一部分，就需要借着神的话经历魂与灵的分开；神的话“是活的，是有功效的，比一切两刃的剑更锋利”─来四12。
陆　“那时，两个人在田里，取去一个，撇下一个。两个女人在磨坊推磨，取去一个，撇下一个”─太二四40～41：
一　两个男人和两个女人，代表主第二次来临时活着的信徒。
二　取去，就是在大灾难前被提─21节，启三10：
1　马太二十四章四十至四十一节，指的是隐密的被提，就是那些预备好且已成熟之人的被提─启十四4下。
2　取去与撇下之人的区别，在于生命的成熟；取去的是活在神圣奥秘的范围里，撇下的是没有活在神圣奥秘的范围里─太二四40～41。
三　主在马太二十四章四十至四十一节的话给我们看见，当我们等候祂来，并期望被提时，我们必须活在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，同时在每天的职责上忠信，过正确平衡的为人生活─参帖后三6～15。

页首-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
LIVING IN THE REALITY OF THE BODY OF CHRIST BY LEARNING CHRIST AS THE REALITY IS IN JESUS
Message Eleven
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living in the Divine and Mystical Realm of the Consummated Spirit
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: John 1:14; 3:3, 5, 13; 7:39; 14:1, 10-11; 16:33; Heb. 4:12; Matt. 24:40-41
I.　The Gospel of John is a mystical book, and the entire record in John is a mystical record of the divine and mystical life, revealing the divine and mystical realm—1:1, 14; 3:3, 5, 13; 14:1; 16:33:
A.　The Gospel of John is a divine and mystical book written by a divine and mystical person to present a vision of the divine and mystical realm of the Triune God and of the consummated Spirit.
B.　All the saints in the Lord's recovery need to have a clear view concerning the physical realm and the divine and mystical realm—Eph. 1:17-23.
C.　We need to enter into a realm that is much higher than the physical realm; this higher realm is the divine and mystical realm.
II.　The Triune God Himself is a divine and mystical realm; the three of the Divine Trinity are self-existing, ever-existing, coexisting, and coinhering, and as such, the Father, the Son, and the Spirit are a divine and mystical realm—John 14:10-11; Matt. 28:19; 2 Cor. 13:14.
III.　We need to live in the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit— John 7:39; Gal. 3:14; Rom. 8:9; 2 Cor. 3:17-18:
A.　The consummated Spirit typified by the compound ointment is the divine and mystical realm, and we should learn to live in this realm—Exo. 30:22-33; 1 John 2:20, 27.
B.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we receive the Spirit as the unique, all-inclusive blessing—Gal. 3:14, 2, 5.
C.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we receive the trans-mission of the ascended Christ and the supply of His heavenly ministry—Eph. 1:22; Heb. 8:1-2.
D.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we experience God's organic salvation—Rom. 5:10.
E.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we live a spontaneous and effortless Christian life according to the automatic function of the law of life— 8:2.
F.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we become divine and mystical persons, living simultaneously in the physical realm and in the divine and mystical realm—John 3:13; Heb. 4:16; 13:13.
G.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we live a life of truthfulness as the expression of the revealed divine reality—2 John 1; 3 John 3; John 4:23-24.
H.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we live in the kingdom of God as the realm of the divine species—3:3, 5.
I.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we live in the divine fellowship; this is the reality of living in the Body of Christ—1 John 1:3, 7; Acts 2:42; Rom. 12:5.
J.　In the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we are mingled with the Triune God for the keeping of the oneness—John 17:21; Eph. 4:3-6:
1.　The genuine oneness is in the Triune God—John 17:21:
a.　The oneness of the believers is actually the oneness of the Triune God.
b.　It is only in the Triune God that we can be perfected into one—v. 23.
2.　The genuine oneness is the mingling of the believers with the Triune God—Eph. 3:14—4:6:
a.　To have this oneness, we must be in the Triune God as the divine and mystical realm.
b.　The believers are one with the Triune God in the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit—Gal. 3:14; Rom. 8:9; 2 Cor. 3:17-18.
IV.　In our experience we actually become part of the divine and mystical realm— John 14:2-3; 15:1, 4; Eph. 4:4-6:
A.　We become part of the divine and mystical realm through regeneration, by which we were born into the divine and mystical realm—John 3:5-6.
B.　We become part of the divine and mystical realm by participating in God's life (v. 15; Col. 3:4), nature (Eph. 1:4; 2 Pet. 1:4), mind (Eph. 4:23; Phil. 2:5), being (2 Cor. 3:18b; Eph. 3:8), image (2 Cor. 3:18a; Rom. 8:29), glory (v. 30; Heb. 2:10), sonship (Eph. 1:5; Rom. 8:23), manifestation (v. 19), and likeness (1 John 3:2).
C.　We become part of the divine and mystical realm by being built up in the Body of Christ, which consummates the New Jerusalem—Eph. 4:16; Rev. 21:2, 10-11:
1.　The Body of Christ is the divine and mystical realm, and the more we are in the reality of the Body of Christ, the more we are in the divine and mystical realm— Rom. 12:4-5; 1 Cor. 12:12-13, 27; Eph. 1:22-23; 4:16.
2.　The Body of Christ consummates the New Jerusalem as the divine and mystical realm in the new heaven and new earth for eternity—Rev. 21:1-2, 10-11.
V.　In order to live in and become part of the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit, we need to experience the dividing of the soul from the spirit by the word of God, which "is living and operative and sharper than any two-edged sword"—Heb. 4:12.
VI.　"At that time two men will be in the field; one is taken and one is left. Two women will be grinding at the mill; one is taken and one is left"—Matt. 24:40-41:
A.　The two men and the two women represent the living believers at the time of the Lord's second coming.
B.　To be taken is to be raptured before the great tribulation—v. 21; Rev. 3:10:
1.　Matthew 24:40-41 refers to the secret rapture, the rapture of the ready ones, the mature ones—Rev. 14:4b.
2.　The difference between the one who is taken and the one who is left is in the maturity of life; one is living in the divine and mystical realm, and the other is not—Matt. 24:40-41.
C.　The Lord's word in Matthew 24:40-41 shows us that as we wait for His coming and expect to be raptured, we must be faithful in our daily duties, living a properly balanced human life while we simultaneously live in the divine and mystical realm of the consummated Spirit—cf. 2 Thes. 3:6-15.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十一篇　活在终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘的范围里，而活在基督身体的实际里
Living in the Reality of the Body of Christ by Living in the Divine and Mystical Realm of the Consummated Spirit
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：约一14，三3，5，13，七39，十四1，10～11，十六33，来四12，太二四40～41
壹　约翰福音是一卷奥秘的书，约翰福音的全部记载也是神圣奥秘生命之奥秘的记载，启示神圣奥秘的范围─一1，14，三3，5，13，十四1，十六33：
I.　The Gospel of John is a mystical book, and the entire record in John is a mystical record of the divine and mystical life, revealing the divine and mystical realm—1:1, 14; 3:3, 5, 13; 14:1; 16:33:
一　约翰福音是由一位神圣奥秘的人所写神圣奥秘的书，陈明三一神与终极完成之灵那神圣奥秘范围的异象。
A.　The Gospel of John is a divine and mystical book written by a divine and mystical person to present a vision of the divine and mystical realm of the Triune God and of the consummated Spirit.
二　主恢复里所有的圣徒，都需要对于物质的范围和神圣奥秘的范围有清楚的看见─弗一17～23。
B.　All the saints in the Lord's recovery need to have a clear view concerning the physical realm and the divine and mystical realm—Eph. 1:17-23.
三　我们需要进入一个范围，是远高于物质的范围；这高得多的范围，就是神圣奥秘的范围。
